//// Obituaries
//
// MP means "multiplayer", as in "multiplayer kill"
//  %o: victim's name
//  %k: killer's name
//  %g: he /she/it, depending on the gender of the victim
//  %h: him/her/it
//  %p: his/her/its

JKE_MP_BALLESTA                 = "%k shoved an exploding arrow through %o.";
JKE_MP_BEAMGUN                  = "%k shot %o with a supersonic explosion.";

// NOTE:
//
// Please keep this in alphabetical order

////
//   ASSORTED
////

///
// None

jkemod/assorted/none                    sounds/assorted/none.ogg

///
// Click

jkemod/assorted/click                   sounds/assorted/click.wav

///
// Generic Explosion

$random jkemod/assorted/explode
{
    jkemod/assorted/explode1
    jkemod/assorted/explode2
    jkemod/assorted/explode3
    jkemod/assorted/explode4
    jkemod/assorted/explode5
}

/home/edrik/projects/jkemod2/pk3/decorate/classes/sorcerer.txt:

actor SorcPlayer: PlayerPawn
{
    Health 100
    ReactionTime 0

    PainChance 255

    Radius 16
    Height 56

    Scale 0.75

    Speed 1

    Player.ColorRange 112, 127

    Player.JumpZ 9.75

    Player.SpawnClass "Mage"
    Player.DisplayName "Sorcerer"
    Player.InvulnerabilityMode "Reflective"
    Player.HealRadiusType "Mana"
    Player.HexenArmor 5, 5, 15, 10, 25

    Player.StartItem " Tri-Staff "
    Player.StartItem " Black Magic "
    Player.StartItem " Fire Gloves "
    Player.StartItem " Hellfist "

    Player.StartItem "JKEMana", 150
    Player.StartItem "FireAmmo", 100
    Player.StartItem "HellFistCounter", 100

    Player.StartItem "IAmAMage"


    States
    {
      Spawn:
        SCPL A -1
        stop

      See:
        SCPL ABCD 4
        loop

      Missile:
      Melee:
        SCPL EF 8
        goto Spawn

      Pain:
        SCPL G 4
        SCPL G 4 A_Pain
        goto Spawn

      Death:
        SCPL H 6
        SCPL I 6 A_PlayerScream
        SCPL JK 6
        SCPL L 6 A_NoBlocking
        SCPL M 6
        SCPL N -1
        stop

      XDeath:
        SCPL O 5 A_PlayerScream
        SCPL P 5
        SCPL R 5 A_NoBlocking
        SCPL STUVW 5
        SCPL X -1
        stop
    }
}


actor IAmAMage: Inventory { +UNDROPPABLE }



/home/edrik/projects/jkemod2/pk3/decorate/delta/railrepeater.txt:

ACTOR RailRepeater: Weapon
{
    Weapon.SelectionOrder 400

    Weapon.AmmoType "Cell"
    Weapon.AmmoGive 100
    Weapon.AmmoUse 1

    Inventory.PickupMessage "$JKE_PK_RAILREPEATER"
    Obituary "$JKE_MP_RAILREPEATER"

    States
    {
      Spawn:
        MINI A -1
        loop

      Ready:
        MING A 9 A_WeaponReady
        Loop

      Deselect:
        TNT1 A 0 A_Lower
        MING A 1 A_Lower
        loop

      Select:
        TNT1 A 0 A_Raise
        MING A 1 A_Raise
        loop

      Fire:
        MING A 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/railrepeater/revup")
        MING HGFEDCB 2
        MING AHGFEDBAHFC 1
        goto Hold

      Hold:
        MINF A 0 A_GunFlash
        MINF A 0
        MINF A 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/railrepeater/hold")
        MINF A 1 bright A_RailAttack(60, 3, 1, "none" , "00 00 FF", 0)
        MING E 1 bright
        MINF B 1 bright A_RailAttack(60, 5, 1, "none" , "00 00 FF", 0)
        MING H 1 bright
        MINF C 1 bright A_RailAttack(60, 2, 1, "none" , "00 00 FF", 0)
        MING C 1 bright
        MING C 0 A_ReFire
        MING A 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/railrepeater/revdown")
        MING CHFDBHGFEDCB 1
        MING HGFEDCB 2
        MING HGFE 3
        MING DCB 4
        Goto Ready
    }
}

/home/edrik/projects/jkemod2/pk3/decorate/tichy/bdw/0_betterfist.txt:


actor " Fists ": DoomWeapon
{
    Weapon.SelectionOrder 3700
    +WEAPON.MELEEWEAPON
    +NOALERT
    +NOAUTOFIRE

    Weapon.SlotNumber 1
    Weapon.SisterWeapon "Power Fists"

    Inventory.PickupMessage "$BDW_PK_FISTS"
    Obituary "$BDW_MP_FISTS"

    States
    {

      Select:
        RPUN A 0 A_TakeInventory("PunchIndicator")
        RPUN A 1 A_Raise
        loop

      Ready:
        RPUN A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("PunchIndicator", 1, "LeftReady")
        goto RightReady

      LeftReady:
        LPUN A 1 A_WeaponReady
        loop

      RightReady:
        RPUN A 1 A_WeaponReady
        loop

      Deselect:
        RPUN A 1 A_JumpIfInventory("PunchIndicator", 1, "LeftDeselect")
        goto RightDeselect

      LeftDeselect:
        LPUN A 1 A_Lower
        loop

      RightDeselect:
        RPUN A 1 A_Lower
        loop

      Fire:
        LPUN A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("PowerBerserkStrength", 1, "BerserkFire")
        LPUN A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("PunchIndicator",  1, "RightJab")
        goto LeftJab

      LeftJab:
        LPUN A 0 A_GiveInventory("PunchIndicator")
        LPUN B 1
        LPUN C 3
        LPUN D 3 A_CustomPunch(2*random(1,10), 1, 0, "FistPunchPuff")
        LPUN EFG 1
        LPUN B 0 A_Jump(12, "ZerkCheck")
        LPUN B 0 A_TakeInventory("TargetHit")
        LPUN B 0 A_ReFire
        goto Ready

      RightJab:
        RPUN A 0 A_TakeInventory("PunchIndicator")
        RPUN B 1
        RPUN C 3
        RPUN D 3 A_CustomPunch(2*random(1,10), 1, 0, "FistPunchPuff")
        RPUN EFG 1
        RPUN B 0 A_Jump(12, "ZerkCheck")
        RPUN B 0 A_TakeInventory("TargetHit")
        RPUN B 0 A_ReFire
        goto Ready



      BerserkFire:
        LPUN A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("PunchIndicator", 1, "BerserkRightJab")
        goto BerserkLeftJab

      BerserkLeftJab:
        LPUN A 0 A_GiveInventory("PunchIndicator")
        LPUN B 1
        LPUN C 3
        LPUN D 3 A_CustomPunch(8*random(1,10), 1, 0, "BerserkPunchPuff")
        LPUN EFG 1
        LPUN B 0 A_Jump(24, "ZerkCheck")
        LPUN B 0 A_TakeInventory("TargetHit")
        LPUN B 0 A_ReFire
        goto Ready

      BerserkRightJab:
        RPUN A 0 A_TakeInventory("PunchIndicator")
        RPUN B 1
        RPUN C 3
        RPUN D 3 A_CustomPunch(8*random(1,10), 1, 0, "BerserkPunchPuff")
        RPUN EFG 1
        RPUN B 0 A_Jump(24, "ZerkCheck")
        RPUN B 0 A_TakeInventory("TargetHit")
        RPUN B 0 A_ReFire
        goto Ready

      AltFire:
        RPUN A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("PunchIndicator", 1, "LeftAlt")
        goto RightAlt

      LeftAlt:
        LPUN A 0 A_TakeInventory("PunchIndicator")
        goto Ready

      RightAlt:
        RPUN A 0 A_GiveInventory("PunchIndicator")
        goto Ready

      ZerkCheck:
        RPUN A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("TargetHit", 1, "RAAAAAGE")
        RPUN A 0 A_TakeInventory("TargetHit")
        RPUN A 0 A_ReFire
        goto Ready

      RAAAAAGE:
        RPUN A 0 ACS_ExecuteAlways(464, 0, 0, 0, 0)
        RPUN A 0 A_TakeInventory("TargetHit")
        RPUN A 0 A_ReFire
        goto Ready
    }
}

/home/edrik/projects/jkemod2/pk3/decorate/tichy/bdw/1_betterchainsaw.txt:

actor " Chainsaw " : Weapon
{
    Weapon.SelectionOrder 2200

    +WEAPON.MELEEWEAPON
    +NOAUTOFIRE
    +NOALERT

    Weapon.SlotNumber 1
    Weapon.SisterWeapon "Power Chainsaw"

    Inventory.PickupMessage "$BDW_PK_CHAINSAW"
    Obituary "$BDW_MP_CHAINSAW"

    States
    {
      Ready:
        SAWG A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ChainsawOn", 1, "ReadyOn")
        goto ReadyOff

      ReadyOff:
        SAWG D 1 A_WeaponReady
        loop

      ReadyOn:
        SAWG C 0 A_PlaySound("betterdoomweapons/sawready", CHAN_WEAPON)
        SAWG C 4 A_WeaponReady
        SAWG C 0 A_AlertMonsters
        SAWG D 4 A_WeaponReady
        SAWG D 0 A_AlertMonsters
        loop


      Deselect:
        SAWG C 1 A_Lower
        loop

      Select:
        SAWG C 0 A_TakeInventory("ChainsawOn")
        SAWG C 1 A_Raise
        loop

      Fire:
        SAWG A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ChainsawOn", 1, "FireOn")
        goto TurnOn

      FireOn:
        SAWG A 0 A_AlertMonsters
        SAWG A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("PowerBerserkStrength", 1, "ZerkSaw")
        goto NormalSaw

        TurnOn:     // the way you aren't
        SAWG A 8 A_GiveInventory("ChainsawOn")
        goto Ready

        TurnOff:     // the way you ARE
        SAWG A 8 A_TakeInventory("ChainsawOn")
        goto Ready

      NormalSaw:
        SAWG AB 3 A_Saw("betterdoomweapons/sawmiss", "betterdoomweapons/sawhit", 2, "SawPuff")
        SAWG A 0 A_Jump(24, "CheckZerk")
        SAWG A 0 A_ReFire
        goto Ready

      ZerkSaw:
        SAWG AB 3 A_Saw("betterdoomweapons/sawmiss", "betterdoomweapons/sawhit", 8, "SawPuff")
        SAWG A 0 A_Jump(48, "CheckZerk")
        SAWG A 0 A_ReFire
        goto Ready


      CheckZerk:
        SAWG A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("TargetHit", 1, "RAAAAAGE")
        SAWG A 0 A_TakeInventory("TargetHit")
        SAWG A 0 A_ReFire
        goto Ready

      RAAAAAGE:
        SAWG A 0 ACS_ExecuteAlways(464, 0, 0, 0, 0)
        SAWG A 0 A_TakeInventory("TargetHit")
        SAWG A 0 A_ReFire
        goto Ready

      AltFire:
        SAWG A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ChainsawOn", 1, "TurnOff")
        goto Ready


      Spawn:
        CSAW A -1
        stop
    }
}


actor "Power Chainsaw" : Weapon
{
    Weapon.SelectionOrder 2200
    Inventory.PickupMessage "BLOOD! BLOOD FOR THE BLOOD GOD!"

    +WEAPON.MELEEWEAPON
    +NOAUTOFIRE
    +NOALERT
    +POWERED_UP

    Weapon.SisterWeapon " Chainsaw "

    Obituary "$BDW_MP_CHAINSAW_POWER"

    States
    {
      Ready:
        SAWG A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ChainsawOn", 1, "ReadyOn")
        goto ReadyOff

      ReadyOff:
        SAWG D 1 A_WeaponReady
        loop

      ReadyOn:
        SAWG C 0 A_StopSound(CHAN_WEAPON)
        SAWG C 0 A_PlaySound("betterdoomweapons/sawready", CHAN_WEAPON)
        SAWG C 4 A_WeaponReady
        SAWG C 0 A_AlertMonsters
        SAWG D 4 A_WeaponReady
        SAWG D 0 A_AlertMonsters
        loop


      Deselect:
        SAWG C 1 A_Lower
        loop

      Select:
        SAWG C 0 A_TakeInventory("ChainsawOn")
        SAWG C 1 A_Raise
        loop

      Fire:
        SAWG A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ChainsawOn", 1, "FireOn")
        goto TurnOn

      FireOn:
        SAWG A 0 A_AlertMonsters
        SAWG A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("PowerBerserkStrength", 1, "ZerkSaw")
        goto NormalSaw

      TurnOn:
        SAWG A 8 A_GiveInventory("ChainsawOn")
        goto Ready

      TurnOff:
        SAWG A 8 A_TakeInventory("ChainsawOn")
        goto Ready

      NormalSaw:
        SAWG AB 3 A_Saw("betterdoomweapons/sawmiss", "betterdoomweapons/sawhit", 5, "SawPuff")
        SAWG A 0 A_Jump(24, "CheckZerk")
        SAWG A 0 A_ReFire
        goto Ready

      ZerkSaw:
        SAWG AB 3 A_Saw("betterdoomweapons/sawmiss", "betterdoomweapons/sawhit", 20, "SawPuff")
        SAWG A 0 A_Jump(48, "CheckZerk")
        SAWG A 0 A_ReFire
        goto Ready


      CheckZerk:
        SAWG A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("TargetHit", 1, "RAAAAAGE")
        SAWG A 0 A_TakeInventory("TargetHit")
        SAWG A 0 A_ReFire
        goto Ready

      RAAAAAGE:
        SAWG A 0 ACS_ExecuteAlways(464, 0, 0, 0, 0)
        SAWG A 0 A_TakeInventory("TargetHit")
        SAWG A 0 A_ReFire
        goto Ready

      AltFire:
        SAWG A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ChainsawOn", 1, "TurnOff")
        goto Ready


      Spawn:
        CSAW A -1
        stop
    }
}

/home/edrik/projects/jkemod2/pk3/decorate/tichy/bdw/2_betterpistol.txt:

actor " Pistol ": DoomWeapon
{
    Weapon.SelectionOrder 1900
    Weapon.AmmoUse1 1
    Weapon.AmmoUse2 4
    Weapon.AmmoGive 20
    Weapon.AmmoType1 "Clip"
    Weapon.AmmoType2 "Clip"

    Weapon.SlotNumber 2
    Weapon.SisterWeapon "Power Pistol"

    +WEAPON.WIMPY_WEAPON
    +NOAUTOFIRE

    Inventory.PickupMessage "$BDW_PK_PISTOL"
    Obituary "$BDW_MP_PISTOL"
    States
    {
      Ready:
        PKPI A 1 A_WeaponReady
        Loop
      Deselect:
        PKPI A 1 A_Lower
        Loop
      Select:
        PKPI A 1 A_Raise
        Loop
      Fire:
        PKPI B    0 A_GunFlash
        PKPI B    0 A_PlaySound("betterdoomweapons/pistolfire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        PKPI B    1 A_FireBullets(1.5, 1, -1, 5, "BulletPuff")
        PKPI CEED 1
        PKPI CB   1 A_WeaponReady
        Goto Ready

      AltFire:
        PKPI B 0 A_GunFlash
        PKPI B 0 A_PlaySound("betterdoomweapons/pistolaltfire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        PKPI B 0 A_FireBullets(5, 3, 4, 5, "BulletPuff")
        PKPI C 1
        PKPI E 12
        PKPI D 3
        PKPI C 2
        PKPI B 1
        PKPI B 0 A_ReFire
        Goto Ready
      Flash:
        PKPF A 1 Bright A_Light1
        goto LightDone

      Spawn:
        PIST A -1
        Stop
    }
}


actor "Power Pistol": DoomWeapon
{
    Weapon.SelectionOrder 1900
    Weapon.AmmoUse1 1
    Weapon.AmmoUse2 4
    Weapon.AmmoGive 20
    Weapon.AmmoType1 "Clip"
    Weapon.AmmoType2 "Clip"

    Weapon.SisterWeapon " Pistol "

    +WEAPON.WIMPY_WEAPON
    +NOAUTOFIRE
    +POWERED_UP

    Inventory.PickupMessage "$BDW_PK_PISTOL"
    Obituary "$BDW_MP_PISTOL_POWER"
    States
    {
      Ready:
        PKPI A 1 A_WeaponReady
        Loop
      Deselect:
        PKPI A 1 A_Lower
        Loop
      Select:
        PKPI A 1 A_Raise
        Loop
      Fire:
        PKPI B    0 A_GunFlash
        PKPI B    0 A_PlaySound("betterdoomweapons/pistolfire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        PKPI B    1 A_FireBullets(0.5, 0.5, -1, 9, "ExplosivePistolBulletPuff")
        PKPI CEED 1
        PKPI CB   1 A_WeaponReady
        Goto Ready

      AltFire:
        PKPI B 0 A_GunFlash
        PKPI B 0 A_PlaySound("betterdoomweapons/pistolaltfire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        PKPI B 0 A_FireBullets(3, 3, 4, 9, "ExplosivePistolBulletPuff")
        PKPI C 1
        PKPI E 8
        PKPI D 3
        PKPI C 2
        PKPI B 1
        PKPI B 0 A_ReFire
        Goto Ready
      Flash:
        PKPF A 1 Bright A_Light1
        goto LightDone

      Spawn:
        PIST A -1
        Stop
    }
}

actor " Shotgun ": DoomWeapon
{
    Weapon.SelectionOrder 1300

    Weapon.AmmoUse1 1
    Weapon.AmmoUse2 2
    Weapon.AmmoGive1  8
    Weapon.AmmoGive2  0
    Weapon.AmmoType1    "Shell"
    Weapon.AmmoType2    "Shell"

    Weapon.SlotNumber 3
    Weapon.SisterWeapon "Power Shotgun"

    Inventory.PickupMessage "$BDW_PK_SHOTGUN"
    Obituary "$BDW_MP_SHOTGUN"

    +NOAUTOFIRE
    +NOALERT

    States
    {
      Ready:
        PKSG A 1 A_WeaponReady
        Loop
      Deselect:
        PKSG A 1 A_Lower
        Loop
      Select:
        PKSG A 1 A_Raise
        Loop

      Fire:
        PKSG A 0 A_AlertMonsters
        PKSG A 0 A_FireBullets(5, 3, 10, 7, "BulletPuff")
        PKSG A 0 A_GunFlash
        PKSG A 7 A_PlaySound("betterdoomweapons/shotfire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        goto GenericPump

      AltFire:
        PKSG A 0 A_AlertMonsters
        PKSG A 0 A_RailAttack(150, 0, 1, "none", "90 90 90", 1, 0, "ShotgunSlugPuff")
        PKSG A 0 A_GunFlash
        PKSG A 11 A_PlaySound("betterdoomweapons/shotfire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        goto GenericPump

      GenericPump:
        PKSG B 3
        PKSG C 2
        PKSG DE 1
        PKSG F 3
        PKSG A 0 A_PlaySound("betterdoomweapons/shotreload", CHAN_WEAPON)
        PKSG F 2
        PKSG G 1
        PKSG H 3
        PKSG G 1
        PKSG F 3
        PKSG E 2
        PKSG DC 1
        PKSG B 3
        PKSG B 0 A_ReFire
        Goto Ready

      Flash:
        SHTF A 4 Bright A_Light1
        SHTF B 3 Bright A_Light2
        Goto LightDone

      AltFlash:
        SHTF A 2 Bright A_Light1
        SHTF B 7 Bright A_Light2
        Goto LightDone
      Spawn:
        SHOT A -1
        Stop
    }
}

actor " Chaingun ": DoomWeapon
{
    Weapon.SelectionOrder 700
    Weapon.AmmoUse1 1
    Weapon.AmmoUse2 1
    Weapon.AmmoGive1 80
    Weapon.AmmoType1 "Clip"
    Weapon.AmmoType2 "Clip"

    Weapon.SisterWeapon "Power Chaingun"

    AttackSound "betterdoomweapons/chaingunfire"

    +AMMO_OPTIONAL
    +ALT_AMMO_OPTIONAL
    +NOALERT

    Inventory.PickupMessage "$BDW_PK_CHAINGUN"
    Obituary "$BDW_MP_CHAINGUN"
    States
    {
      Ready:
        PKCG A 1 A_WeaponReady
        Loop
      Deselect:
        PKCG A 1 A_Lower
        Loop
      Select:
        PKCG A 1 A_Raise
        Loop


////
////    Begin Fire + Alt Fire
////
      Fire:
        PKCG A 0 A_JumpIfNoAmmo("Rev")
        PKCG A 0 A_GunFlash
        PKCG A 0 ACS_ExecuteAlways(474, 0, 0,40)
        PKCG A 0 A_AlertMonsters
        PKCG A 1 bright A_FireBullets(2, 2, -1, 8, "BulletPuff")
        PKCG BD 1 bright
        PKCG A 1 A_JumpIfInventory("MainFired", 1, "Hold")
        PKCG B 2 A_WeaponReady
        PKCG C 3 A_WeaponReady
        PKCG D 4 A_WeaponReady
        Goto Ready

      Rev:
        PKCG ABD 1
        PKCG A 1 A_JumpIfInventory("MainFired", 1, "Hold")
        PKCG B 2 A_WeaponReady
        PKCG C 3 A_WeaponReady
        PKCG D 4 A_WeaponReady
        Goto Ready

      Hold:
        PKCG A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired", 1, "AltFire7")
        goto Fire

      AltFire:

      AltRev0:
        PKCG D 0 A_JumpIfInventory("MainFired", 1, "AltFire0")
        PKCG A 4
        PKCG B 4
        PKCG C 4
        PKCG D 4
        PKCG D 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired",  1, "AltRev1")
        goto Ready

        PKCG D 0 A_JumpIfInventory("MainFired", 1, "AltFire1")

        PKCG B 4

        goto AltRev1

      AltRev3:
        PKCG D 0 A_JumpIfInventory("MainFired", 1, "AltFire3")
        PKCG A 3
        PKCG B 3
        PKCG C 2
        PKCG D 2
        PKCG D 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired",  1, "AltRev4")
        goto AltRev2

      AltRev4:
        PKCG D 0 A_JumpIfInventory("MainFired", 1, "AltFire4")
        PKCG A 2
        PKCG B 2
        PKCG C 2
        PKCG D 2
        PKCG D 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired",  1, "AltRev5")
        goto AltRev3

      AltRev5:
        PKCG D 0 A_JumpIfInventory("MainFired", 1, "AltFire5")
        PKCG A 2
        PKCG B 2
        PKCG C 1
        PKCG D 1
        PKCG D 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired",  1, "AltRev6")
        goto AltRev4

      AltRev6:
        PKCG D 0 A_JumpIfInventory("MainFired", 1, "AltFire6")
        PKCG A 1
        PKCG B 1
        PKCG C 1
        PKCG D 1
        PKCG D 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired",  1, "AltRev7")
        goto AltRev5

      AltRev7:
        PKCG D 0 A_JumpIfInventory("MainFired", 1, "AltFire7")
        PKCG A 1
        PKCG C 1
        PKCG D 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired",  1, "AltRev8")
        goto AltRev7Special

      AltRev8:
        PKCG D 0 A_JumpIfInventory("MainFired", 1, "AltFire8")
        PKCG A 1
        PKCG C 1
        PKCG D 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired",  1, "AltRev9")

      AltRev9:
        PKCG D 0 A_JumpIfInventory("MainFired", 1, "AltFire9")

        PKCG C 1
        PKCG D 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired",  1, "AltRev10")

        goto AltRev9

        PKCG D 0 A_JumpIfNoAmmo(1)
        goto AltRev5
        PKCG A 2
        PKCG B 2
        PKCG C 1
        PKCG D 1
        PKCG D 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired",  1, "AltDown6")
        goto AltDown4

      AltDown6:
        PKCG D 0 A_JumpIfNoAmmo(1)
        goto AltRev6
        PKCG A 1
        PKCG B 1
        PKCG C 1
        PKCG D 1
        PKCG D 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired",  1, "AltDown7")
        goto AltDown5

      AltDown7:
        PKCG D 0 A_JumpIfNoAmmo(1)
        goto AltRev7
        PKCG A 1
        PKCG C 1
        PKCG D 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired",  1, "AltDown8")
        goto AltDown7Special

      AltDown8:
        PKCG D 0 A_JumpIfNoAmmo(1)
        goto AltRev8
        PKCG A 1
        PKCG C 1
        PKCG D 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired",  1, "AltDown9")
        goto AltDown7

      AltDown9:

        goto AltRev9
        PKCG A 1
        PKCG C 1
        PKCG D 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired",  1, "AltDown10")

      AltDown10:

    AltRev7Special:
        PKCG D 0 A_JumpIfInventory("MainFired", 1, "Fire")
        goto AltRev6

    AltFire7Special:
        PKCG D 0 A_JumpIfInventory("MainFired", 1, "Fire")
        goto AltFire6

    AltDown7Special:
        PKCG D 0 A_JumpIfInventory("MainFired", 1, "Rev")
        goto AltDown6

////
////    End Fire + Alt Fire
////



      Flash:
      AltFlash:
        TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(128,4)
        PKCF A 2 bright A_Light2
        PKCF B 1 bright
        TNT1 A 2
        Goto LightDone
        PKCF A 2 bright A_Light1
        PKCF B 1 bright A_Light1
        TNT1 A 2 A_Light1
        Goto LightDone


      AltFlash:
        PKCF A 1 A_Light2
        goto LightDone

      Spawn:
        MGUN A -1
        Stop
    }
}

Actor " B-Rocket Launcher ": DoomWeapon
{
    Weapon.SelectionOrder 800
    Weapon.AmmoType1 "RocketAmmo"
    Weapon.AmmoType2 "RocketAmmo"
    Weapon.AmmoUse1  1
    Weapon.AmmoUse2  5
    Weapon.AmmoGive1 2
    +NOAUTOAIM
    +NOAUTOFIRE

    Weapon.SlotNumber 5
    Weapon.SisterWeapon "Power Rocket Launcher"

    Inventory.PickupMessage "$BDW_PK_ROCKETLAUNCHER"
    States
    {
      Ready:
        PKRL A 1 A_WeaponReady
        Loop
      Deselect:
        PKRL A 1 A_Lower
        Loop
      Select:
        PKRL A 1 A_Raise
        Loop
      Fire:
        PKRL A 2
        PKRL A 4 A_GunFlash
        PKRL B 2
        PKRL D 0 A_PlaySound("betterdoomweapons/rocketfire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        PKRL D 3 A_FireCustomMissile("BetterRocket")
        PKRL C 3
        PKRL BE 2
        PKRL FG 1
        PKRL A 0 A_ReFire
        Goto Ready
      AltFire:
        PKRL A 2
        PKRL A 4 A_GunFlash
        PKRL B 1
        PKRL D 0 A_PlaySound("betterdoomweapons/rocketaltfire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        PKRL D 0 A_Recoil(6)
        PKRL D 0  A_FireCustomMissile("BetterTinyRocket", -15, 0, -6, 0, 0,  0)
        PKRL D 0  A_FireCustomMissile("BetterTinyRocket",  15, 0,  6, 0, 0,  0)
        PKRL D 0  A_FireCustomMissile("BetterTinyRocket",  -5, 0, -3, 0, 2,  3)
        PKRL D 0  A_FireCustomMissile("BetterTinyRocket",   5, 0,  3, 0, 2,  3)
        PKRL D 0  A_FireCustomMissile("BetterTinyRocket",  -5, 0, -3, 0, 2, -3)
        PKRL D 0  A_FireCustomMissile("BetterTinyRocket",   5, 0,  3, 0, 2, -3)
        PKRL D 0  A_FireCustomMissile("BetterTinyRocket",   2, 0, -6, 0, 0,  0)
        PKRL D 0  A_FireCustomMissile("BetterTinyRocket",  -2, 0,  6, 0, 0,  0)
        PKRL D 0  A_FireCustomMissile("BetterTinyRocket",   0, 0,  0, 0, 0,  2)
        PKRL D 18 A_FireCustomMissile("BetterTinyRocket",   0, 1,  0, 0, 0, -2)
        PKRL C 6
        PKRL B 4
        PKRL E 2
        PKRL FG 1
        PKRL A 0 A_ReFire
        Goto Ready
      Flash:
        PKRF A 3 Bright A_Light1
        PKRF B 2 Bright
        PKRF C 2 Bright A_Light2
        PKRF DE 3 Bright
        Goto LightDone
      Flash:
        PKRF A 3 Bright A_Light1
        PKRF B 2 Bright
        PKRF C 2 Bright A_Light2
        PKRF DE 3 Bright
        Goto LightDone
      Spawn:
        LAUN A -1
        Stop
    }
}

        PKRL D 0 A_PlaySound("betterdoomweapons/rocketfire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        PKRL B 1 A_FireCustomMissile("BetterPowerRocket")
        PKRL D 5
        PKRL B 4
        PKRL E 2
        PKRL FG 1
        PKRL A 0 A_ReFire
        Goto Ready
      AltFire:
        PKRL B 0 A_GunFlash
        PKRL D 0 A_PlaySound("betterdoomweapons/rocketaltfire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        PKRL D 0 A_Recoil(6)
        PKRL D 0  A_FireCustomMissile("BetterPowerTinyRocket", -15, 0, -6, 0, 0,  0)
        PKRL D 0  A_FireCustomMissile("BetterPowerTinyRocket",  15, 0,  6, 0, 0,  0)
        PKRL D 0  A_FireCustomMissile("BetterPowerTinyRocket",  -5, 0, -3, 0, 2,  3)
        PKRL D 0  A_FireCustomMissile("BetterPowerTinyRocket",   5, 0,  3, 0, 2,  3)
        PKRL D 0  A_FireCustomMissile("BetterPowerTinyRocket",  -5, 0, -3, 0, 2, -3)
        PKRL D 0  A_FireCustomMissile("BetterPowerTinyRocket",   5, 0,  3, 0, 2, -3)
        PKRL D 0  A_FireCustomMissile("BetterPowerTinyRocket",   2, 0, -6, 0, 0,  0)
        PKRL D 0  A_FireCustomMissile("BetterPowerTinyRocket",  -2, 0,  6, 0, 0,  0)
        PKRL D 0  A_FireCustomMissile("BetterPowerTinyRocket",   0, 0,  0, 0, 0,  2)
        PKRL B 1  A_FireCustomMissile("BetterPowerTinyRocket",   0, 1,  0, 0, 0, -2)
        PKRL C 1
        PKRL D 12
        PKRL C 6
        PKRL B 4
        PKRL E 2
        PKRL FG 1
        PKRL A 0 A_ReFire
        Goto Ready
      Flash:
        PKRF B 1 Bright A_Light1
        PKRF C 2 Bright A_Light2
        PKRF DE 3 Bright
        Goto LightDone
      AltFlash:
        PKRF B 1 Bright A_Light1
        PKRF C 1 Bright A_Light2
        PKRF DE 6 Bright
        Goto LightDone
      Spawn:
        LAUN A -1
        Stop
    }
}

ACTOR " B-Plasma Rifle ": DoomWeapon
{
    Weapon.SelectionOrder 100
    Weapon.AmmoUse1  1
    Weapon.AmmoUse2  4
    Weapon.AmmoGive1   80
    Weapon.AmmoGive2   20
    Weapon.AmmoType1     "Cell"
    Weapon.AmmoType2     "Cell"

    Weapon.SlotNumber 6
    Weapon.SisterWeapon "Power Plasma Rifle"

    +NOAUTOFIRE

    Inventory.PickupMessage "$BDW_PK_PLASMARIFLE"

    States
    {
      Ready:
        PKPL AAAAAAAA 1 A_WeaponReady
        PKPL A 0 A_GiveInventory("PlasmaCounter", 1)
        Loop
      Deselect:
        PKPL A 0 A_GiveInventory("PlasmaCounter", 30)
        PKPL A 1 A_Lower
        Loop
      Select:
        PKPL A 1 A_Raise
        Loop

      Fire:
        PKPL A 0 A_GunFlash
        PKPL A 3 A_FireCustomMissile("BetterPlasma")
        PKPL B 0 A_ReFire

        PKPL B 3
        PKPL C 2
        PKPL D 12
        PKPL C 2
        PKPL BA 1
        Goto Ready

      AltFire:
        PKPL A 0 A_GunFlash
        PKPL A 4 A_FireCustomMissile("BetterRipperPlasma")
        PKPL B 0 A_ReFire

        PKPL B 3
        PKPL C 2
        PKPL D 12
        PKPL C 2
        PKPL BA 1
        Goto Ready


      Flash:
        PLSF B 3 Bright A_Light1
        PLSF A 3 Bright A_Light1
        TNT1 A 1 Bright A_Light1
        Goto LightDone

      AltFlash:
        YLSF B 4 Bright A_Light1
        YLSF A 4 Bright A_Light1
        TNT1 A 1 Bright A_Light1
        Goto LightDone
      Spawn:
        PLAS A -1
        Stop
    }
}

actor BFGCounter: Inventory

    inventory.amount 1

actor " BFG9000 ": DoomWeapon
{
    Weapon.SelectionOrder 2800
    Weapon.AmmoUse1  40
    Weapon.AmmoUse2  1
    Weapon.AmmoGive1    40
    Weapon.AmmoGive2    40
    Weapon.AmmoType1       "Cell"
    Weapon.AmmoType2       "Cell"

    Weapon.SisterWeapon "Power BFG9000"

    +NOAUTOFIRE
    +NOAUTOAIM

    Inventory.PickupMessage "$BDW_PK_BFG9000"
    Obituary "$BDW_MP_BFG9000SPLASH"
    States
    {
      Ready:
        BBFG A 1 A_WeaponReady
        loop
      Deselect:
        BBFG A 1 A_Lower
        loop
      Select:
        BBFG A 1 A_Raise
        loop

      Fire:
        BBFG B 30 bright        A_PlaySound("betterdoomweapons/bfgfire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        BBFG B 0                A_GunFlash
        BBFG B 0                A_FireCustomMissile("BetterBFGBall")
        BBFG B 1 bright offset(0, 36)
        BBFG B 2 bright offset(0, 40)
        BBFG C 7 bright offset(0, 32) A_Recoil(4)
        BBFG C 1 bright offset(0, 26) A_ReFire
        BBFG C 3 bright
        BBFG B 4 bright offset(0, 32)
        goto Ready

      Hold:
        BBFG C 1 bright offset(0, 26) A_PlaySound("betterdoomweapons/bfgfire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        BBFG C 3 bright
        BBFG B 4 bright offset(0, 32)
        BBFG B 22 bright
        goto Fire+1

      AltFire:
        BBFG A 30               A_PlaySound("betterdoomweapons/bfgfire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        BBFG B 0                A_GunFlash
        BBFG B 0                A_FireCustomMissile("BetterBFGPlasma1", random(-5, 5), 1, random(-6, 6), random(-6, 6), 0, random(-2, 2) )
        BBFG B 1 bright offset(0, 36) A_FireCustomMissile("BetterBFGPlasma2", random(-5, 5), 0, random(-6, 6), random(-6, 6), 0, random(-2, 2) )
        BBFG B 0                A_FireCustomMissile("BetterBFGPlasma1", random(-5, 5), 1, random(-6, 6), random(-6, 6), 0, random(-2, 2) )
        BBFG B 1 bright offset(0, 36) A_FireCustomMissile("BetterBFGPlasma2", random(-5, 5), 0, random(-6, 6), random(-6, 6), 0, random(-2, 2) )

      AltFireLoop:
        BBFG B 0 A_GiveInventory("BFGCounter", 1)
        BBFG B 0 A_FireCustomMissile("BetterBFGPlasma1", random(-5, 5), 1, random(-6, 6), random(-6, 6), 0, random(-2, 2) )
        BBFG B 1 bright offset(0, 40) A_FireCustomMissile("BetterBFGPlasma2", random(-5, 5), 0, random(-6, 6), random(-6, 6), 0, random(-2, 2) )
        BFGG B 0 A_JumpIfInventory("BFGCounter", 38, "AltFireEnd")
        loop

      AltFireEnd:
        BBFG B 0 A_TakeInventory("BFGCounter")
        BBFG B 8 bright offset(0, 40)
        BBFG B 3 bright offset(0, 38)
        BBFG B 3 bright offset(0, 34)
        goto Ready

      Flash:
        BBFF A  3 bright A_Light1
        BBFF B  7 bright A_Light2
        BBFF C  4 bright A_Light1
        BBFF DE 6 bright
        Goto LightDone

      Spawn:
        BBFG Z -1
        stop
    }
}

actor IAmTheBetterPlayer: Inventory { +UNDROPPABLE inventory.maxamount 1 }


actor BetterPlayer: PlayerPawn
{
    Speed 1
    Health 100
    Radius 16
    Height 56
    Mass 100
    PainChance 255

    Player.ColorRange 112, 127

    Player.DisplayName "Doomguy"
    Player.JumpZ 9

    Player.SpawnClass "Mage"
    Player.HexenArmor 10, 50, 10, 30, 10
    Player.HealRadiusType "Health"
    Player.InvulnerabilityMode "Ghost"

    Player.StartItem "IAmTheBetterPlayer"

    Player.StartItem "Clip",  200
    Player.StartItem "Shell", 50
    Player.StartItem "RocketAmmo", 50
    Player.StartItem "Cell", 300

    // ordered by each weapon's usefulness for me

    Player.StartItem " B-Super Shotgun "
    Player.StartItem " B-Plasma Rifle "
    Player.StartItem " Chaingun "
    Player.StartItem " B-Rocket Launcher "
    Player.StartItem " Pistol "
    Player.StartItem " Shotgun "
    Player.StartItem " Chainsaw "
    Player.StartItem " Fists "

    Player.CrouchSprite "BPLC"

    States
    {
      Spawn:
        BPLY A -1
        Loop
      See:
        BPLY ABCD 4
        Loop
      Missile:
        BPLY E 12
        Goto Spawn
      Melee:
        BPLY F 6 BRIGHT
        Goto Missile
      Pain:
        BPLY G 4
        BPLY G 4 A_Pain
        Goto Spawn
      Death:
        BPLY H 0 A_PlayerSkinCheck("AltSkinDeath")
      Death1:
        BPLY H 10
        BPLY I 10 A_PlayerScream
        BPLY J 10 A_NoBlocking
        BPLY KLM 10
        BPLY N -1
        Stop
      XDeath:
        BPLY O 0 A_PlayerSkinCheck("AltSkinXDeath")
      XDeath1:
        BPLY O 5
        BPLY P 5 A_XScream
        BPLY Q 5 A_NoBlocking
        BPLY RSTUV 5
        BPLY W -1
        Stop
      AltSkinDeath:
        BPLY H 6
        BPLY I 6 A_PlayerScream
        BPLY JK 6
        BPLY L 6 A_NoBlocking
        BPLY MNO 6
        BPLY P -1
        Stop
      AltSkinXDeath:
        BPLY Q 5 A_PlayerScream
        BPLY R 0 A_NoBlocking
        BPLY R 5 A_SkullPop
        BPLY STUVWX 5
        BPLY Y -1
        Stop
    }

}

/home/edrik/projects/jkemod2/pk3/decorate/tichy/strifemarine/01_knife.txt:

actor " S-Knife ": Weapon
{
    Weapon.SlotNumber 1
    +WEAPON.WIMPY_WEAPON
    +WEAPON.MELEEWEAPON
    +NOEXTREMEDEATH
    +NOALERT
    +NOAUTOFIRE

    DamageType HexenMarine
    Weapon.SelectionOrder 2500

    Inventory.PickupMessage "$STRIFEMARINE_PK_DWEAPKNIFE"
    Obituary "$STRIFEMARINE_MP_DWEAPKNIFE"

    States
    {
      Spawn:
        HXNF A -1
        loop
      Ready:
        HXKN A 1 A_WeaponReady
        loop
      Deselect:
        HXKN AA 0 A_Lower
        HXKN A 1 A_Lower
        loop
      Select:
        HXKN AA 0 A_Raise
        HXKN A 1 A_Raise
        loop
      Fire:
        HXKN B 1
        HXKN C 1 A_CustomPunch(15*random(1,3), 1, 0, "HKnifePuff")
        HXKN DEF 1
        HXKN ED 4
        HXKN A 2 A_ReFire
        goto Ready


      AltFire:
        HXKN A 4 Offset(-11, 50)
        HXKN C 2 Offset(6, 70)
        HXKN D 3 Offset(38, 35)
        HXKN D 7 Offset(35, 41)
        HXKN D 1 Offset(33, 27)
        HXKN D 1 Offset(29, 7)
        HXKN D 0 A_CustomPunch(1, 1, 0, "HKnifePuff", 96)
        HXKN DDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDDD 0 A_CustomPunch(1, 1, 0, "HInvisibleKnifePuff", 96)
        HXKN D 6 Offset(25, -13)
        HXKN D 4 Offset(26, -6)
        HXKN D 1 Offset(29, 7)
        HXKN D 1 Offset(33, 27)
        HXMN D 0 A_Refire
        HXKN D 7 Offset(35, 41)
        HXKN D 4 Offset(38, 35)
        HXKN C 3 Offset(6, 70)
        HXKN A 2 Offset(-11, 50)
        goto Ready

      AltHold:
        HXKN D 3 Offset(33, 27)
        goto AltFire+4
    }
}

ACTOR DWeapEnforcer: Weapon
{
    Weapon.SlotNumber 2

    Weapon.AmmoType1 "Clip"
    Weapon.AmmoType2 "Clip"
    Weapon.AmmoUse1 1
    Weapon.AmmoUse2 1
    Weapon.AmmoGive1 24

    Weapon.Kickback 100

    Weapon.SelectionOrder 2000
    Weapon.UpSound "hexenmarine/enforcerup"
    Decal "BulletChip"
    Scale 0.4


    Inventory.PickupMessage "$STRIFEMARINE_PK_DWEAPENFORCER"
    Obituary "$STRIFEMARINE_MP_DWEAPENFORCER"

    States
    {
      Spawn:
        ENFC Z -1
        Loop
      Ready:
        ENFC A 1 A_WeaponReady
        Loop
      Deselect:
        ENFC AA 0 A_Lower
        ENFC A 1 A_Lower
        Loop
      Select:
        ENFC A 12
      Select2:
        ENFC AA 0 A_Raise
        ENFC A 1 A_Raise
        Loop
      Fire:
        ENFS A 0 A_GunFlash
        ENFS A 0 A_PlaySound("hexenmarine/enforcerfire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        ENFS A 0 A_FireBullets (2, 2, 1, 7, "HBulletPuff")
        ENFS AB 1 BRIGHT
        ENFC CEDCBA 1
        ENFC A 4
        ENFC A 0 A_ReFire
        Goto Ready
      AltFire:
        ENFS A 0 A_GunFlash
        ENFS A 0 A_PlaySound("hexenmarine/enforcerfire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        ENFS A 0 A_FireBullets (6, 6, -1, 7, "HBulletPuff")
        ENFS AB 1 BRIGHT
        ENFC CEDCBA 1
        ENFC A 0 A_ReFire
        Goto Ready
      Flash:
        TNT1 A 2 A_Light2
        TNT1 A 1 A_Light1
        TNT1 A 0 A_Light0
        Stop
    }
}



/home/edrik/projects/jkemod2/pk3/decorate/tichy/strifemarine/03_shotgun.txt:

actor " S-Shotgun ": Weapon
{
    Weapon.SelectionOrder 1500
    Weapon.SlotNumber 3

    Weapon.AmmoType1 "Shell"
    Weapon.AmmoType2 "Shell"
    Weapon.AmmoUse1 1
    Weapon.AmmoUse2 1
    Weapon.AmmoGive 8

    Inventory.PickupMessage "$STRIFEMARINE_PK_DWEAPSHOTGUN"
    Obituary "$STRIFEMARINE_MP_DWEAPSHOTGUN"

    Decal "BulletChip"
    States
    {
      Ready:
        HMSG A 1 A_WeaponReady
        Loop
      Deselect:
        HMSG A 1 A_Lower
        Loop
      Select:
        HMSG A 1 A_Raise
        Loop


      Fire:
        HMSG B 0 A_CheckReload
        HMSG B 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ShellsPumped", 1, "Fire2")
        goto FirePump

      FirePump:
        HMSG F 0 A_GiveInventory("ShellsPumped")
        HMSG FGH 1
        HMSG I 2 A_PlaySoundEx("hexenmarine/shotreload", "SoundSlot5")
        HMSG JKLKJI 2
        HMSG HGF 1
        goto Fire2

      Fire2:
        HMSG A 0 A_TakeInventory("ShellsPumped")
        HMSG A 0 A_AlertMonsters
        HMSG A 0 A_PlaySound("hexenmarine/shotfire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        HMSG A 0 A_FireBullets(2, 2, 10, 6, "HBulletPuff")
        HMSG D 1  bright
        HMSG ED 2 bright
        HMSG CB 1 bright
        HMSG A 0 A_CheckReload
        goto FirePump2

      FirePump2:
        HMSG F 0 A_GiveInventory("ShellsPumped")
        HMSG FGH 1
        HMSG I 2 A_PlaySoundEx("hexenmarine/shotreload", "SoundSlot5")
        HMSG JKLKJ 2
        HMSG K 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired", 1, "AltHold")
        HMSG I 2
        HMSG HGF 1
        HMSG A 0 A_ReFire
        goto Ready


      AltFire:
        HMSG B 0 A_CheckReload
        HMSG B 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Shell", 2, 1)
        goto Fire
        HMSG B 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ShellsPumped", 2, "AltFire2")
        HMSG B 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ShellsPumped", 1, "AltFire1Pump")
        goto AltFire2Pump

      AltFire1Pump:
        HMSG F 0 A_GiveInventory("ShellsPumped")
        HMSG FGH 1
        HMSG I 2 A_PlaySoundEx("hexenmarine/shotreload", "SoundSlot5")
        HMSG JKLKJI 2
        HMSG HGF 1
        goto AltFire2

      AltFire2Pump:
        HMSG F 0 A_GiveInventory("ShellsPumped", 2)
        HMSG FGH 1
        HMSG I 2 A_PlaySoundEx("hexenmarine/shotreload", "SoundSlot5")
        HMSG JKLKJ 2
        HMSG I 0 A_PlaySoundEx("hexenmarine/shotreload", "SoundSlot5")
        HMSG JKLKJI 2
        HMSG HGF 1
        goto AltFire2

      AltFire2:
        HMSG A 0 A_TakeInventory("ShellsPumped")
        HMSG A 0 A_AlertMonsters
        HMSG A 0 A_PlaySound("hexenmarine/shotdoublefire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        HMSG AA 0 A_FireBullets(2, 2, 10, 6, "HBulletPuff")
        HMSG D 1  bright
        HMSG ED 2 bright
        HMSG CB 1 bright
        HMSG A 0 A_CheckReload
        goto AltFirePump2

      AltFirePump2:
        HMSG A 3
        HMSG F 0 A_GiveInventory("ShellsPumped")
        HMSG FGH 1
        HMSG I 2 A_PlaySoundEx("hexenmarine/shotreload", "SoundSlot5")
        HMSG JKLKJ 2
        HMSG I 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired", 1, "AltHold")
        HMSG I 2
        HMSG HGF 1
        HMSG A 0
        goto Ready

      AltHold:
        HMSG I 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Shell", 2, "AltHoldPump")
        HMSG I 0 A_CheckReload // just in case
        HMSG I 2
        HMSG HGF 1
        HMSG A 0
        goto Ready

      AltHoldPump:
        HMSG I 0 A_PlaySoundEx("hexenmarine/shotreload", "SoundSlot5")
        HMSG JKLKJI 2
        HMSG HGF 1
        goto AltFire2

      Flash:
        TNT1 A 4 Bright A_Light1
        TNT1 A 3 Bright A_Light2
        Goto LightDone
      Spawn:
        HMSG Z -1
        Stop
    }
}


actor ShellsPumped: Inventory
{
    inventory.maxAmount 2
    +UNDROPPABLE
}



/home/edrik/projects/jkemod2/pk3/decorate/tichy/strifemarine/04_chaingun.txt:

actor " S-Chaingun ": Weapon
{
    Weapon.AmmoType1 "Clip"
    Weapon.AmmoType2 "Clip"
    Weapon.AmmoUse1 1
    Weapon.AmmoUse2 1
    Weapon.AmmoGive 50

    AttackSound "hexenmarine/chaingunfire"
    Decal "BulletChip"

    Inventory.PickupMessage "$STRIFEMARINE_PK_DWEAPCHAINGUN"
    Obituary "$STRIFEMARINE_MP_DWEAPCHAINGUN"

    States
    {
      Spawn:
        HXCG Z -1
        Loop
      Ready:
        HXCG A 1 A_WeaponReady
        Loop
      Deselect:
        HXCG A 0 A_StopSound(CHAN_BODY)
        HXCG A 0 A_Lower
        HXCG A 1 A_Lower
        Goto Deselect
      Select:
        HXCG A 0 A_Raise
        HXCG A 1 A_Raise
        Goto Select

      Fire:
        HXCG F 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Clip", 1, 1)
        goto Empty
        HXCG F 1 bright A_FireBullets(1, 1, -1, 6, "HBulletPuff")
        HXCG B 2
        HXCG F 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Clip", 1, 1)
        goto Empty
        HXCG G 1 bright A_FireBullets(1, 1, -1, 6, "HBulletPuff")
        HXCG DEE 1
        HXCG E 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired", 1, "AF3")
        HXCG E 0 A_Refire
        HXCG A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired", 1, "AF3")
        HXCG A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("MainFired", 1, "Fire")

        HXCG B 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired", 1, "AF30")
        HXCG B 1 A_JumpIfInventory("MainFired", 1, "Fire")

        HXCG C 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired", 1, "AF3")
        HXCG C 1 A_JumpIfInventory("MainFired", 1, "Fire")

        HXCG D 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired", 1, "AF20")
        HXCG D 2 A_JumpIfInventory("MainFired", 1, "Fire")

        HXCG E 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired", 1, "AF21")
        HXCG E 2 A_JumpIfInventory("MainFired", 1, "Fire")

        HXCG A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired", 1, "AF2")
        HXCG A 2 A_JumpIfInventory("MainFired", 1, "Fire")

        HXCG B 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired", 1, "AF10")
        HXCG B 3 A_JumpIfInventory("MainFired", 1, "Fire")

        HXCG C 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired", 1, "AF11")
        HXCG C 3 A_JumpIfInventory("MainFired", 1, "Fire")

        HXCG D 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired", 1, "AF00")
        HXCG D 4 A_JumpIfInventory("MainFired", 1, "Fire")

        HXCG E 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired", 1, "AF01")
        HXCG E 5 A_JumpIfInventory("MainFired", 1, "Fire")

        goto Ready

      AltFire:
        HXCG A 0 A_PlaySound("hexenmarine/chaingunup")
      AF0:
        HXCG F 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Clip", 1, 1)
        goto Empty
        HXCG A 0 A_AlertMonsters
        HXCG F 2 bright A_FireBullets(0.5, 0.5, -1, 6, "HBulletPuff")
        HXCG A 2
        HXCG B 4
        HXCG F 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Clip", 1, 1)
        goto Empty
        HXCG A 0 A_AlertMonsters
        HXCG G 2 bright A_FireBullets(0.5, 0.5, -1, 6, "HBulletPuff")
        HXCG C 2
      AF00:
        HXCG D 3
      AF01:
        HXCG E 4
        HXCG F 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired", 1, "AF1")
        goto EF0

      AF1:
        HXCG F 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Clip", 1, 1)
        goto Empty
        HXCG A 0 A_AlertMonsters
        HXCG F 2 bright A_FireBullets(1, 1, -1, 6, "HBulletPuff")
      AF10:
        HXCG B 2
      AF11:
        HXCG F 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Clip", 1, 1)
        goto Empty
        HXCG A 0 A_AlertMonsters
        HXCG G 2 bright A_FireBullets(1, 1, -1, 6, "HBulletPuff")
        HXCG D 2
        HXCG E 2
        HXCG F 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired", 1, "AF2")
        HXCG F 0 A_JumpIfInventory("MainFired", 1, "Fire")
        goto EF1

      AF2:
        HXCG F 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Clip", 1, 1)
        goto Empty
        HXCG A 0 A_AlertMonsters
        HXCG F 1 bright A_FireBullets(2, 2, -1, 6, "HBulletPuff")
        HXCG B 1
        HXCG F 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Clip", 1, 1)
        goto Empty
        HXCG A 0 A_AlertMonsters
        HXCG G 1 bright A_FireBullets(2, 2, -1, 6, "HBulletPuff")
        HXCG D 1
      AF20:
        HXCG E 1
      AF21:
        HXCG F 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired", 1, "AF3")
        HXCG F 0 A_JumpIfInventory("MainFired", 1, "Fire")
        goto EF2

      AF3:
        HXCG A 0 A_PlaySound("hexenmarine/chaingunrev", CHAN_BODY, 1.0, true)
        HXCG F 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Clip", 1, 1)
        goto Empty

      AF30:
        HXCG F 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Clip", 1, 1)
        goto Empty

        HXCG G 1 bright A_FireBullets(3, 3, -1, 6, "HBulletPuff")
        HXCG E 1
        HXCG F 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired", 1, "AF4")

      AF4:

        HXCG G 1 bright A_FireBullets(5, 5, -1, 6, "HBulletPuff")
        HXCG F 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired", 1, "AF6")
        goto EF4

      AF6:

    Height 12
    Speed 40
    Damage (15*(random(10,30)/10))
    Gravity 0.3
    Scale 0.5
    Projectile
    -NOGRAVITY

        stop
      Death:
        MISL B 0 Bright A_ChangeFlag("NoGravity", 1)
        MISL B 6 Bright A_Explode(64, 64)
        MISL CD 6 Bright
        Stop
    }

        PLSB A 0 A_PlaySound("hexenmarine/beamfire", CHAN_WEAPON)

        PLSB A 0 A_PlaySound("hexenmarine/beamfire", CHAN_WEAPON)

        PLSB A 0 A_PlaySound("hexenmarine/beamfire", CHAN_WEAPON)

        PLSB A 0 A_PlaySound("hexenmarine/beamprojstop", CHAN_WEAPON)

      Flash:

        PLSB C 3 bright A_Light2

        Stop
    }

        INGN B 5
        INGN A 50
        goto Ready

      AltFire:
        INGN B 3
        INGN C 6 A_FireBullets(0,0, 1,0, "IonBeacon2")
        INGN B 5
        INGN A 25
        goto Ready

      Spawn:
        WEP8 ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOP 2 bright
        loop
    }
}

/home/edrik/projects/jkemod2/pk3/decorate/weapons/ballesta.txt:

Actor Ballesta: Weapon
{
    Weapon.SelectionOrder 560
    Weapon.AmmoUse 1
    Weapon.AmmoGive 30
    Weapon.AmmoType "BallestaAmmo"
    Weapon.upsound "weapons/load2"
    Inventory.PickupMessage "$JKE_PK_BALLESTA"
    Obituary "$JKE_MP_BALLESTA"
    States
    {
      Ready:
        XBOW H 1 A_WeaponReady
        Loop
      Deselect:
        XBOW H 1 A_Lower
        Loop
      Select:
        XBOW H 1 A_Raise
        Loop
      Fire:
        XBOW B 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/ballesta/fire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        XBOW B 4 bright A_FireCustomMissile("BallestaArrow", 0, 1)
        XBOW F 4
        XBOW J 3
        XBOW I 3 A_ReFire
        Goto Ready
      Spawn:
        CBOW A -1
        Stop
    }
}


actor BallestaArrow
{
    Radius 5
    Height 5
    Gravity 0.25

    Projectile
    +EXPLODEONWATER
    +DEHEXPLOSION

    Damage 20
    Speed 70

    DeathSound "jkemod/ballesta/explode"

    States
    {
      Spawn:
        ARRW A -1
        stop

      Death:
        CFCF Q 0 A_Explode(32, 64, 0)
        CFCF QRSTUVWXYZ 2
        stop
    }
}



/home/edrik/projects/jkemod2/pk3/decorate/weapons/beamgun.txt:

actor BeamGunCounter: Ammo
{
    +IGNORESKILL
    Inventory.MaxAmount 8
}

actor " Beam Gun ": Weapon
{
    +AMMO_OPTIONAL
    +NOALERT
    Weapon.AmmoGive1 7
    Weapon.AmmoGive2 7
    Weapon.AmmoType1 "BeamGunCounter"
    Weapon.AmmoType2 "BeamAmmo"
    Weapon.AmmoUse1 1
    Weapon.SelectionOrder 780

    Inventory.PickupMessage "$JKE_PK_BEAMGUN"
    Obituary "$JKE_MP_BEAMGUN"
    States
    {
      Select:
        BMGN A 1 A_Raise
        loop
      Deselect:
        BMGN A 1 A_Lower
        loop

      Ready:
        BMGN A 1 A_WeaponReady
        Loop

      Fire:
        BMGN A 0 A_JumpIfNoAmmo("AltFire")

        BMGN A 35 A_PlaySound("jkemod/beamgun/charge", CHAN_WEAPON)

      ReFire:
        BMGN L 0 A_AlertMonsters
        BMGN L 0 A_Light2
        BMGN L 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/beamgun/fire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        BMGN L 0 A_RailAttack(400, 2, 0, "EF 60 00", "FF FF 00", 1, 0)
        BMGN L 0 A_FireBullets(0, 0, 1, 0, "BeamGunPuff")
        BMGN L 1 bright offset(4,  35)
        BMGN L 3 bright offset(12, 41)
        BMGN A 3 A_Light0
        BMGN A 2 offset(10, 40)
        BMGN A 1 offset(8, 38)
        BMGN A 1 offset(6, 37)
        BMGN A 1 offset(4, 35)
        BMGN A 1 offset(2, 34)
        BMGN A 8 offset(-1, 32)
        BMGN A 0 A_ReFire
        goto Ready

      Hold:
        BMGN A 0 A_JumpIfNoAmmo("AltFire")
        goto ReFire


      AltFire:
        BMGN A 0 A_ClearRefire
        BMGN A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("BeamGunCounter", 0, "NoReload")
        BMGN A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("BeamAmmo", 1, "ReloadStart")
        goto NoReload

      ReloadStart:
        BMGN B 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/beamgun/load1", CHAN_WEAPON)
        BMGN BCDEFG 1
        BMGN HIJ 2
        BMGN K 12
        BMGN K 9 A_PlaySound("jkemod/beamgun/load2", CHAN_WEAPON)
        goto ReloadLoop

      ReloadLoop:
        BMGN A 0 A_TakeInventory("BeamAmmo", 1)
        BMGN A 0 A_GiveInventory("BeamGunCounter", 1)
        BMGN A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("BeamGunCounter", 0, "ReloadEnd")
        BMGN A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("BeamAmmo", 1, "ReloadLoop")
        goto ReloadEnd

      ReloadEnd:
        BMGN JIH 2
        BMGN G 2 A_PlaySound("jkemod/beamgun/load3", CHAN_WEAPON)
        BMGN FEDCBA 1
        BMGN A 4
        goto Ready

      NoReload:
        BMGN A 1
        BMGN A 0 A_ReFire
        goto Ready

      Spawn:
        BMGN M -1
        stop
    }
}

actor BeamGunPuff: BulletPuff
{
    VSpeed 0
    RenderStyle Add

    +PUFFONACTORS
    +PUFFGETSOWNER

    States
    {
      Spawn:
        TNT1 A 0
        TNT1 A 0 A_Explode(192, 160, 0)
        MISL BBBBCCCDD 2 bright
        Stop
    }
}

        BSCL A 1

        stop

actor " BFG7000 ": Weapon

    Weapon.AmmoType1 "Cell"

    Weapon.AmmoGive1 150
    Weapon.SelectionOrder 520
    Weapon.yadjust -10

    Inventory.PickupMessage "$JKE_PK_BFG7000"
    Obituary "$JKE_MP_BFG7000"
    States
    {
      Ready:
        BFGZ C 1 A_WeaponReady
        Loop
      Select:
        BFGZ C 1 A_Raise
        Loop
      Deselect:
        BFGZ C 1 A_Lower
        Loop
      Fire:
        BFGZ D 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/bfg7000/load", CHAN_WEAPON)
        BFGZ DEDEDEDEDEDEDEDE 2
        BFGZ E 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/bfg7000/fire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        BFGZ E 2 bright A_Light1
        BFGZ FEFEFEFGGGG 2 bright

        BFGZ G 0 bright A_GunFlash
        BFGZ H 4 bright A_FireCustomMissile("BFG7000Ball", 0, 1, 6)
        BFGZ I 4 A_Light0
        BFGZ C 105
        goto Ready
      Spawn:
        BFGZ Z -1
        stop
    }
}

/home/edrik/projects/jkemod2/pk3/decorate/weapons/blackmagic.txt:

actor " Black Magic ": Weapon
{
    +UNDROPPABLE
    +ALT_AMMO_OPTIONAL
    +NOALERT

    Weapon.AmmoType1 "JKEMana"
    Weapon.AmmoType2 "JKEMana"
    Weapon.AmmoUse1 25
    Weapon.AmmoUse2 125
    Weapon.AmmoGive1 300

    Weapon.SelectionOrder 910

    Inventory.PickupMessage "$JKE_PK_BLACKMAGIC"

    Obituary "$JKE_MP_BLACKMAGIC_MELEEc"

    States
    {

      Select:
        BLMG A 0 A_Raise
        BLMG A 1
        loop

      Deselect:
        BLMG B 0 A_TakeInventory("InAltFire")
        BLMG A 0 ACS_ExecuteAlways(874, 0, 0, 0, 0)
        BLMG A 1 A_Lower
        loop

      Ready:
        BLMG A 1 A_WeaponReady
        Loop

      Fire:
        BLMG H 0 A_AlertMonsters
        BLMG H 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/blackmagic/charge", CHAN_WEAPON)
        BLMG HIJIJIJIJIJ 3 bright
        BLMG KL 5 bright
        BLMG H 0 A_AlertMonsters
        BLMG M 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/blackmagic/charge", CHAN_WEAPON)
        BLMG MNMNMN 3 bright
        BLMG H 0 A_AlertMonsters
        BLMG N 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/blackmagic/hold", CHAN_WEAPON)
        BLMG OPQR 2 bright
        BLMG R 0 A_ReFire
        goto FireEnd

      Hold:
        BLMG H 0 A_AlertMonsters
        BLMG N 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/blackmagic/hold", CHAN_WEAPON)
        BLMG OPQR 2 bright A_CustomPunch(13+random(0, 6), 1, 0, "Bulletpuff", 0)
        BLMG A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired", 1, "NeverMind")
        BLMG R 0 A_ReFire
        goto FireEnd

      FireEnd:
        BLMG STU 3 bright
        BLMG U 0 bright A_FireCustomMissile("BlackMagicShot")
        BLMG VHI 3 bright
        goto Ready

      NeverMind:
        BLMG A 0 A_ClearRefire
        BLMG NMLKJI 3 bright
        BLMG A 12
        goto Ready

      AltFire:
        BLMG B 0 A_GiveInventory("InAltFire")
        BMLG B 0 A_GunFlash
        BLMG B 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/startflame", CHAN_WEAPON)
        BLMG B 0 bright ACS_ExecuteAlways(874, 0, 1, 0, 0)
        BLMG BCBCBC 3 bright
        goto AltLoop

      AltLoop:
        BLMG A 0 A_GiveInventory("JKEMana", 1)
        BLMG BB 1 bright A_JumpIfInventory("MainFired", 1, "Blast")
        BLMG A 0 A_GiveInventory("JKEMana", 1)
        BLMG A 0 A_GiveInventory("FireAmmo", 1)
        BLMG BC 1 bright A_JumpIfInventory("MainFired", 1, "Blast")
        BLMG A 0 A_GiveInventory("JKEMana", 1)
        BLMG CC 1 bright A_JumpIfInventory("MainFired", 1, "Blast")
        BLMG C 0 HealThing(1)
        BLMG C 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired", 1, "AltLoop")
        goto AltEnd


      NoBlast:
        BLMG A 0 A_GiveInventory("JKEMana", 1)
        BLMG BB 1 bright
        BLMG A 0 A_GiveInventory("JKEMana", 1)
        BLMG A 0 A_GiveInventory("FireAmmo", 1)
        BLMG BC 1 bright
        BLMG A 0 A_GiveInventory("JKEMana", 1)
        BLMG CC 1 bright
        BLMG C 0 HealThing(1)
        BLMG C 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired", 1, "AltLoop")
        goto AltEnd

      AltEnd:
        BLMG A 0 ACS_ExecuteAlways(874, 0, 0, 0, 0)
        BLMG B 3 bright
        BLMG B 0 A_TakeInventory("InAltFire")
        BLMG A 12
        goto Ready

      Blast:
        BLMG A 0 A_JumpIfNoAmmo("NoBlast")

        BLMG H 0 A_AlertMonsters
        BLMG DE 3 bright
        BLMG F 3 bright
        BLMG G 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/blackmagic/altfire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        BLMG G 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/blackmagic/altfire", CHAN_BODY)
        BLMG G 0 A_FireCustomMissile("BlackMagicAltShot", 0, 1, -6)
        BLMG G 0 A_FireCustomMissile("BlackMagicAltShot", 0, 0, 6)
        BLMG G 3 bright
        BLMG FE 3 bright
        goto AltLoop

      AltFlash:
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BlackMagicFlameExplosion")


        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BlackMagicFlame", 96, 0, 0, 0,0,0, 0)
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BlackMagicFlame", 96, 0, 0, 0,0,0, 5)
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BlackMagicFlame", 96, 0, 0, 0,0,0, 10)
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BlackMagicFlame", 96, 0, 0, 0,0,0, 15)
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BlackMagicFlame", 96, 0, 0, 0,0,0, 20)
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BlackMagicFlame", 96, 0, 0, 0,0,0, 25)

        DEVG A 2 A_Light0
        DEVG A 0 A_ReFire
        goto Ready


      Spawn:

        stop
    }

/home/edrik/projects/jkemod2/pk3/decorate/weapons/dualberettas.txt:

actor " Dual Berettas ": Weapon
{
    Scale 0.2

    +AMMO_OPTIONAL
    +NOALERT

    weapon.AmmoGive1 60
    Weapon.AmmoGive2 60
    weapon.AmmoType1 "BerettaCounter"
    Weapon.AmmoType2 "BerettaAmmo"
    weapon.AmmoUse1 1

    weapon.selectionorder 400

    Inventory.PickupMessage "$JKE_PK_DUALBERETTAS"
    Obituary "$JKE_MP_DUALBERETTAS"
    states
    {
      Select:
        BRTU AAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_Raise
        BRTU B 2
        BRTU C 2
        BRTU D 2
        BRTU E 2
        BRTU F 2 A_PlaySound("jkemod/dualberettas/up", CHAN_WEAPON)
        BRTU F 12 A_GunFlash
        Goto Ready

      Deselect:
        BRT2 A 1 A_Lower
        loop

        Flash:     // NOT ACTUALLY A GUN FLASH
        BR2U A 2
        BR2U B 2
        BR2U C 2
        BR2U D 2
        BR2U E 2
        BR2U F 2
        Goto LightDone

      Ready:
        BRT2 A 1 A_WeaponReady
        loop

      Fire:
        BRT2 A 0 A_JumpIfNoAmmo("Reload")
        BRT2 A 0 A_AlertMonsters
        BRT2 A 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/dualberettas/fire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        BRT2 A 0 A_FireBullets(2, 1, -1, 9, "BulletPuff", 1)

        BRT2 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("BerettaSide", 1, "LeftFire")
        goto RightFire

      RightFire:
        BRT2 B 3 bright A_GiveInventory("BerettaSide")
        BRT2 C 2 bright A_FireCustomMissile("PistolCasing", 50, 0, 6, -4)
        BRT2 C 0 A_ReFire
        BRT2 D 2
        goto Ready

      LeftFire:
        BRT2 F 3 bright A_TakeInventory("BerettaSide")
        BRT2 G 2 bright A_FireCustomMissile("PistolCasing", -50, 0, -6, -4)
        BRT2 G 0 A_ReFire
        BRT2 H 2
        goto Ready


      Hold:
        BRT2 A 0 A_JumpIfNoAmmo("Reload")
        BRT2 A 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/dualberettas/fire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        BRT2 A 0 A_FireBullets(2, 1, -1, 9, "BulletPuff", 1)

        BRT2 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("BerettaSide", 1, "LeftHold")
        goto RightHold

      RightHold:
        BRT2 E 3 bright A_GiveInventory("BerettaSide")
        BRT2 C 2 bright A_FireCustomMissile("PistolCasing", 50, 0, 6, -4)
        BRT2 C 0 A_ReFire
        BRT2 D 2
        goto Ready

      LeftHold:
        BRT2 I 3 bright A_TakeInventory("BerettaSide")
        BRT2 G 2 bright A_FireCustomMissile("PistolCasing", -50, 0, -6, -4)
        BRT2 G 0 A_ReFire
        BRT2 H 2
        goto Ready




      AltFire:
        BRR2 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("BerettaCounter", 0, "NoReload")

      Reload:
        BRR2 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("BerettaAmmo", 1, "ReloadStart")
        Goto NoReload

      ReloadStart:
        BRR2 A 2
        BRR2 B 2 A_PlaySound("jkemod/assorted/click", CHAN_WEAPON)
        BRR2 CDEF 2
        BRR2 G 2 A_PlaySound("jkemod/dualberettas/out", CHAN_WEAPON)
        BRR2 HI 2
        BRR2 J 2 A_PlaySound("jkemod/dualberettas/load1", CHAN_WEAPON)
        BRR2 K 4 A_PlaySound("jkemod/dualberettas/load2", CHAN_WEAPON)
        BRR2 LMN 2
        BRTR ABCDEFG 2
        BRTR J 2 A_PlaySound("jkemod/dualberettas/load1", CHAN_WEAPON)
        BRTR K 4 A_PlaySound("jkemod/dualberettas/load2", CHAN_WEAPON)

      ReloadLoop:
        BRTR K 0 A_TakeInventory("BerettaAmmo", 1)
        BRTR K 0 A_GiveInventory("BerettaCounter", 1)
        BRTR K 0 A_JumpIfInventory("BerettaCounter", 0, "ReloadEnd")
        BRTR K 0 A_JumpIfInventory("BerettaAmmo", 1, "ReloadLoop")
        goto ReloadEnd

      ReloadEnd:
        BRT2 A 3
        Goto Ready

      NoReload:
        BRT2 A 1
        BRT2 A 0 A_ReFire
        goto Ready

      Spawn:
        1337 A -1
        stop
    }
}

    +IGNORESKILL
    Inventory.MaxAmount 30
}

    Inventory.MaxAmount 1
    +UNDROPPABLE

      Select:
        FIST A 1 A_Raise
        loop

      Deselect:
        FIST A 1 A_Lower
        loop

      Ready:
        FIST A 1 A_WeaponReady
        Loop

      Fire:
        FIST B 0 A_Recoil(-3)
        FIST B 2
        FIST B 0 A_Recoil(-4)

      SplodyLoop:
        FIST C 0 A_GiveInventory("SplodyCounter")
        FIST C 0 A_Recoil(-4)
        FIST C 0 A_FireCustomMissile("ExpFuTrail", 0, 0, 0, 0)
        FIST C 1 A_CustomPunch(6, 0, 0, "Bulletpuff", 0)

        FIST C 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SplodyCounter", 0, "Fire2")
        goto SplodyLoop

      Fire2:
        FIST C 0 A_TakeInventory("SplodyCounter")
        FIST B 0 A_Recoil(-4)
        FIST C 1 A_CustomPunch(6, 0, 0, "Bulletpuff", 0)
        FIST B 0 A_Recoil(-4)
        FIST C 1 A_CustomPunch(6, 0, 0, "Bulletpuff", 0)
        FIST B 0 A_Recoil(-4)
        FIST C 1 A_CustomPunch(6, 0, 0, "Bulletpuff", 0)


        FIST BA 2
        KICK AB 2


        KICK C 2 ThrustThingZ(0, 40, 0, 0)
        KICK DDDDD 1 A_CustomPunch(6, 0, 0, "Bulletpuff", 0)
        KICK D 0 A_FireCustomMissile("ExpFuKick", 0, 0, 0, 0)
        KICK DDDDD 1 A_CustomPunch(6, 0, 0, "Bulletpuff", 0)
        KICK CBA 2
        FIST D 2


        FIST E 0 ThrustThing(angle*256/360, 50, 1, 0)
        FIST EEE 1 A_CustomPunch(6, 0, 0, "Bulletpuff", 0)
        FIST E 0 A_FireCustomMissile("ExpFuFire", 0, 0, 0, 5, 0)
        FIST EEEEEEEEEEEEE 1 A_CustomPunch(6, 0, 0, "Bulletpuff", 0)


        FIST DA 2
        goto Ready


      Spawn:
        BLMG WXYZ 8 bright
        loop
    }
}

actor " Fire SSG ": Weapon

    Weapon.AmmoType2 "Shell"

    {

        loop

        loop

        FSH2 A 1 A_WeaponReady
        loop

      Fire:
        FSH2 A 0        A_GunFlash

        FSH2 AAAAAAAAAA 0 A_FireCustomMissile("FireSSGShot1", random(-150, 150)/10.0, 0, -5, 0, 0, random(-70, 70)/10.0)

        FSH2 A 2 offset(0, 40) bright
        FSH2 A 2 offset(0, 36) bright
        FSH2 B 6
        FSH2 C 5
        FSH2 D 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/firessg/open", CHAN_WEAPON)
        FSH2 D 6
        FSH2 E 0 A_FireCustomMissile("ShellCasing", 30, 0, 0, 7)
        FSH2 E 0 A_FireCustomMissile("ShellCasing", 33, 0, 0, 7)
        FSH2 E 7
        FSH2 F 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/firessg/load", CHAN_WEAPON)
        FSH2 F 6
        FSH2 G 5
        FSH2 H 5
        FSH2 A 2 A_ReFire
        FSH2 A 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/firessg/close", CHAN_WEAPON)
        Goto Ready
      AltFire:
        FSH2 A 0 A_GunFlash
        FSH2 A 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/firessg/fire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        FSH2 A 0 A_FireCustomMissile("FireSSGShot2", 0, 1, 4, 0)
        FSH2 A 2 offset(0, 33) bright A_Recoil(4)
        FSH2 A 2 offset(0, 40) bright

        FSH2 A 0 A_GunFlash
        FSH2 A 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/firessg/fire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        FSH2 A 0 A_FireCustomMissile("FireSSGShot2", 0, 1, -4, 0)
        FSH2 A 2 offset(0, 33) bright A_Recoil(4)
        FSH2 A 2 offset(0, 40) bright
        FSH2 A 2 offset(0, 36) bright
        FSH2 B 6
        FSH2 C 5
        FSH2 D 4 A_PlaySound("jkemod/firessg/open", CHAN_WEAPON)
        FSH2 E 0 A_FireCustomMissile("ShellCasing", 30, 0, 0, 7)
        FSH2 E 0 A_FireCustomMissile("ShellCasing", 33, 0, 0, 7)
        FSH2 E 7

        FSH2 G 4
        FSH2 H 5
        FSH2 A 2 A_ReFire
        FSH2 A 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/firessg/close", CHAN_WEAPON)
        Goto Ready

      Flash:

/home/edrik/projects/jkemod2/pk3/decorate/weapons/fmodminigun.txt:

actor " FMod Minigun ": Weapon
{
    Weapon.AmmoType2 "MinigunAmmo"
    Weapon.AmmoUse2 1
    Weapon.AmmoGive2 100

    +NOALERT
    Weapon.SelectionOrder 550

    AttackSound "jkemod/fmodminigun/fire"

    Inventory.PickupMessage "$JKE_PK_FMODMINIGUN"
    Obituary "$JKE_MP_FMODMINIGUN"

    States
    {

      Select:
        D3CG A 1 A_Raise
        loop

      Deselect:
        D3CG A 1 A_Lower
        loop

      Ready:
        D3CG A 1 A_WeaponReady
        Loop

      Fire:
        D3CG A 1
        D3CG A 0 A_ReFire
        goto Ready

      AltFire:
        D3CG B 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/fmodminigun/up", CHAN_WEAPON)
        D3CG BA 6
        D3CG BA 5
        D3CG BA 4
        D3CG BA 3
        D3CG BA 2
        D3CG BA 1
        D3CG A 0 A_ReFire
        goto Down

      AltHold:
        D3CG A 0 ACS_Execute(876, 0, 1, 0, 0)
        D3CG A 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/fmodminigun/spin", CHAN_WEAPON)
        D3CG BABABA 1 A_JumpIfInventory("MainFired", 1, "Shoot")
        D3CG A 0 A_ReFire
        goto Down

      Shoot:
        D3CG A 0 A_AlertMonsters
        D3CG A 0 ACS_ExecuteAlways(876, 0, 0, 20, 0)
        D3CG A 0 Radius_Quake(2, 3, 0, 1, 0)
        D3CG A 0 A_GunFlash

        D3CF A 0 A_FireCustomMissile("AssaultCasing", random(-400, -700)/10.0, 0, 3, 3)
        D3CG A 1 bright A_FireBullets(5, 5, 1, 10, "BulletPuff")

        D3CF A 0 A_FireCustomMissile("AssaultCasing", random(-400, -700)/10.0, 0, 3, 3)
        D3CG B 1 bright A_FireBullets(5, 5, 1, 10, "BulletPuff")

        D3CG A 0 A_JumpIfNoAmmo("Down")
        D3CG A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired", 1, 1)
        goto Down

        D3CG A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("MainFired", 1, "Shoot")
        D3CG A 0 A_ReFire
        goto Down

      Down:
        D3CG A 0 ACS_Execute(876, 0, 1, 0, 0)
        D3CG BA 1 A_ReFire
        D3CG BA 2 A_ReFire
        D3CG A 2 A_PlaySound("jkemod/fmodminigun/down", CHAN_WEAPON)
        D3CG BA 3 A_ReFire
        D3CG BA 4
        D3CG BA 5
        D3CG BA 6
        goto Ready

      AltFlash:
        D3CF A 0 A_Jump(255, "AltFlash1", "AltFlash2", "AltFlash3", "AltFlash4")

      AltFlash1:
        D3CF A 2 bright A_Light1
        D3CF A 0 A_Light0
        goto LightDone

      AltFlash2:
        D3CF B 2 bright A_Light1
        D3CF A 0 A_Light0
        goto LightDone

      AltFlash3:
        D3CF C 2 bright A_Light1
        D3CF A 0 A_Light0
        goto LightDone

      AltFlash4:
        D3CF D 2 bright A_Light1
        D3CF A 0 A_Light0
        goto LightDone

      Spawn:
        D3CG Z -1
        stop
    }
}

actor FragmentShard
{
    Projectile
    +PUFFGETSOWNER
    Height 3
    Radius 3
    Speed 40
    Scale 0.5
    Damage (3)
    Obituary "$JKE_MP_FRAGMENTLAUNCHER2"
    States
    {
      Spawn:
        FSHD ABC 3
        loop
      Death:
        TNT1 A 0
        stop
    }
}

actor Fragmentlauncher: Weapon
{
    weapon.AmmoGive 10
    weapon.AmmoType1 "ExplosiveAmmo"
    weapon.AmmoType2 "ExplosiveAmmo"
    weapon.AmmoUse1 1
    weapon.AmmoUse2 1
    weapon.selectionorder 460
    Inventory.PickupMessage "$JKE_PK_FRAGMENTLAUNCHER"
    states
    {
      Ready:
        FLAK A 1 A_WeaponReady
        Loop
      Select:
        FLAK A 1 A_Raise
        Loop
      Deselect:
        FLAK A 1 A_Lower
        Loop

      Fire:
        FLAK B 0 A_FireCustomMissile("FragmentChunk", 0, 1, 0, 0)
        FLAK B 0 A_FireCustomMissile("FragmentChunk", 3, 0, 0, 0)
        FLAK B 0 A_FireCustomMissile("FragmentChunk", 6, 0, 0, 0)
        FLAK B 0 A_FireCustomMissile("FragmentChunk", -3, 0, 0, 0)
        FLAK B 0 A_FireCustomMissile("FragmentChunk", -7, 0, 0, 0)
        FLAK B 0 A_FireCustomMissile("FragmentChunk", 9, 0, 0, 0)
        FLAK B 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/fragmentlauncher/fire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        FLAK B 4 bright A_Light1
        FLAK C 4 bright
        goto GenericReload

      AltFire:
        FLAK B 0 A_FireCustomMissile("FragmentShell", 0, 1, 0, 0)
        FLAK B 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/fragmentlauncher/fire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        FLAK B 4 bright A_Light1
        FLAK C 4 bright
        goto GenericReload

      GenericReload:
        FLAK C 0 A_Light0
        FLAK A 5 A_CheckReload
        FLAK D 4 A_PlaySound("jkemod/fragmentlauncher/open", CHAN_WEAPON)
        FLAK E 4
        FLAK F 4
        FLAK G 4
        FLAK H 4 A_PlaySound("jkemod/fragmentlauncher/load", CHAN_WEAPON)
        FLAK I 4
        FLAK J 4
        FLAK A 1 A_ReFire
        Goto Ready

      Spawn:
        FLAK Z -1
        stop
    }
}



/home/edrik/projects/jkemod2/pk3/decorate/weapons/ghettoblaster.txt:

actor " Ghetto Blaster ": DoomWeapon
{
    Weapon.SelectionOrder 200

    Inventory.PickupMessage "$JKE_PK_GHETTOBLASTER"
    Obituary "$JKE_MP_GHETTOBLASTER"

    Scale 0.5

    States
    {
      Select:
        GBLS A 1 A_Raise
        Loop

      Deselect:
        GBLS A 0 A_StopSoundEx("SoundSlot6")
        goto Deselect2

      Deselect2:
        GBLS A 1 A_Lower
        loop

      Ready:
        GBLS A 0 A_StopSoundEx("SoundSlot6")
        GBLS A 1 A_WeaponReady
        loop

      Fire:
        GBLS A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("jkemod/ghettoblaster/rickroll", "SoundSlot6", 1)
        GBLS A 1 A_FireCustomMissile("GhettoRickroll")
        GBLS A 0 A_Refire
        goto Ready


      AltFire:
        GBLS A 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/ghettoblaster/explode", CHAN_WEAPON)
        GBLS A 0 A_FireCustomMissile("GhettoExplosion")
        GBLS A 210
        goto Ready

      Spawn:
        GBLS B -1
        Stop
    }
}

    Radius 1
    Height 1

    Projectile
    Damage 0

    +FORCERADIUSDMG
    +NODAMAGETHRUST
}

        stop

/home/edrik/projects/jkemod2/pk3/decorate/weapons/handshotgun.txt:

actor " Hand Shotgun ": Weapon
{
    Weapon.AmmoType "Shell"
    Weapon.AmmoUse 1
    Weapon.AmmoGive 8

    Weapon.SelectionOrder 2000


    Inventory.PickupMessage "$JKE_PK_HANDSHOTGUN"
    Obituary "$JKE_MP_HANDSHOTGUN"

    States
    {
      Select:
        SSS4 A 0 A_Raise
        SSS4 A 1 A_Raise
        loop
      Deselect:
        SSS4 A 0 A_Lower
        SSS4 A 1 A_Lower
        loop

      Ready:
        SSS4 A 1 A_WeaponReady
        Loop

      Fire:
        SSS4 A 0 A_GunFlash
        SSS5 A 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/handshotgun/fire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        SSS4 A 6 bright A_FireBullets(8, 8, 10, 5, "Bulletpuff", 1)
        SSS4 A 8
        SSS4 D 4
        SSS4 E 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/handshotgun/open", CHAN_WEAPON)
        SSS4 E 3
        SSS4 E 0 A_FireCustomMissile("ShellCasing", 30, 0, 0, 7)
        SSS4 E 5
        SSS4 F 5
        SSS4 G 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/handshotgun/load", CHAN_WEAPON)
        SSS4 G 5
        SSS4 A 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/handshotgun/close", CHAN_WEAPON)
        SSS4 D 7
        SSS4 A 1 A_ReFire
        SSS4 A 3
        goto Ready

      Flash:
        SSF4 A 3 bright
        SSF4 B 3 bright
        goto LightDone

      Spawn:
        SSS4 Z -1
        stop
    }
}

actor " Heavy Chaingun ": Weapon
{
    Game Doom
    Weapon.SelectionOrder 360
    Weapon.AmmoUse1 1
    Weapon.AmmoUse2 2
    Weapon.AmmoGive 80
    Weapon.AmmoType1 "Clip"
    Weapon.AmmoType2 "Clip"
    weapon.upsound "jkemod/heavychaingun/up"
    Inventory.PickupMessage "$JKE_PK_HEAVYCHAINGUN"
    Obituary "$JKE_MP_HEAVYCHAINGUN"
    States
    {
      Ready:
        CHG2 A 1 A_WeaponReady
        Loop

      Deselect:
        CHG2 A 1 A_Lower
        Loop

      Select:
        CHG2 A 1 A_Raise
        Loop

      Fire:
        CHG2 A 35 A_PlaySound("jkemod/heavychaingun/load", CHAN_WEAPON)

        CHG2 B 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/heavychaingun/fire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        CHG2 B 0 A_Recoil(0.2)
        CHG2 B 0 A_FireBullets(5, 5, 1, 7, "BulletPuff", 1)
        CHG2 B 0 A_FireCustomMissile("AssaultCasing", 47, 0, 0, 7)
        CHG2 B 4 bright A_Light1

        CHG2 C 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/heavychaingun/fire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        CHG2 C 0 A_Recoil(0.2)
        CHG2 B 0 A_FireBullets(5, 5, 1, 7, "BulletPuff", 1)
        CHG2 B 0 A_FireCustomMissile("AssaultCasing", 47, 0, 0, 7)
        CHG2 C 4 bright A_Light0

        CHG2 B 0 A_ReFire
        goto End

      Hold:
        CHG2 B 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/heavychaingun/fire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        CHG2 B 0 A_Recoil(0.4)
        CHG2 B 0 A_FireBullets(5, 5, 1, 7, "BulletPuff", 1)
        CHG2 B 0 A_FireCustomMissile("AssaultCasing", 47, 0, 0, 7)
        CHG2 B 2 bright A_Light1

        CHG2 C 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/heavychaingun/fire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        CHG2 C 0 A_Recoil(0.2)
        CHG2 B 0 A_FireBullets(5, 5, 1, 7, "BulletPuff", 1)
        CHG2 B 0 A_FireCustomMissile("AssaultCasing", 47, 0, 0, 7)
        CHG2 C 2 bright A_Light0

        CHG2 B 0 A_ReFire
        goto End


      AltFire:
        CHG2 A 35 A_PlaySound("jkemod/heavychaingun/load", CHAN_WEAPON)

        CHG2 B 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/heavychaingun/altfire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        CHG2 B 0 A_Recoil(0.4)
        CHG2 B 0 A_FireBullets(5, 5, 2, 7, "BulletPuff", 1)
        CHG2 B 0 A_FireCustomMissile("AssaultCasing", 47, 0, 0, 7)
        CHG2 B 4 bright A_Light1

        CHG2 C 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/heavychaingun/altfire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        CHG2 C 0 A_Recoil(0.4)
        CHG2 B 0 A_FireBullets(5, 5, 2, 7, "BulletPuff", 1)
        CHG2 B 0 A_FireCustomMissile("AssaultCasing", 47, 0, 0, 7)
        CHG2 C 4 bright A_Light0

        CHG2 B 0 A_ReFire
        goto End

      AltHold:
        CHG2 B 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/heavychaingun/altfire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        CHG2 B 0 A_Recoil(0.4)
        CHG2 B 0 A_FireBullets(5, 5, 2, 7, "BulletPuff", 1)
        CHG2 B 0 A_FireCustomMissile("AssaultCasing", 47, 0, 0, 7)
        CHG2 B 2 bright A_Light1

        CHG2 C 0 A_Recoil(0.4)
        CHG2 B 0 A_FireBullets(5, 5, 2, 7, "BulletPuff", 1)
        CHG2 B 0 A_FireCustomMissile("AssaultCasing", 47, 0, 0, 7)
        CHG2 C 2 bright A_Light0

        CHG2 B 0 A_ReFire
        goto End

      End:
        CHG2 A 2
        CHG2 D 27
        Goto Ready
      Spawn:
        CHG2 Z -1
        Stop
    }

        BHND E 1 bright
        BHND D 3 bright
        goto Ready

      Spawn:
        TNT1 A 0
        stop
    }

actor " J-Pistol ": Weapon
{
    +AMMO_OPTIONAL
    +NOALERT
    weapon.AmmoGive1 28
    weapon.AmmoType1 "JPistolCounter"
    weapon.AmmoType2 "Clip"
    weapon.AmmoGive2 40
    weapon.AmmoUse1 1
    weapon.selectionorder 1200

    Inventory.PickupMessage "$JKE_PK_JPISTOL"
    Obituary "$JKE_MP_JPISTOL"
    states
    {
      Ready:
        PIS3 A 1 A_WeaponReady
      Select:
        PIS3 A 0 A_Raise
        PIS3 A 1 A_Raise
        loop
      Deselect:
        PIS3 A 0 A_Lower
        PIS3 A 1 A_Lower
        loop
      Fire:
        PIS3 A 0 A_JumpIfNoAmmo("AltFire")

        PIS3 B 0 A_AlertMonsters
        PIS3 B 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/jpistol/fire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        PIS3 B 2 bright A_FireBullets(2, 2, 1, 6, "Bulletpuff", 1)

        PIS3 C 3 bright
        PIS3 D 4 A_FireCustomMissile("PistolCasing", -45, 0, 6, 0)
        PIS3 A 0 A_ReFire
        goto Ready

      AltFire:
        PIS3 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("JPistolCounter", 0, "NoReload")
        PIS3 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Clip", 1, "ReloadStart")
        goto NoReload

      ReloadStart:
        PIS3 C 2 offset(0, 40)
        PIS3 C 2 offset(0, 50) A_PlaySound("jkemod/assorted/click", CHAN_WEAPON)
        PIS3 C 2 offset(0, 60)
        PIS3 C 30 offset(0, 70)

      ReloadLoop:
        PIS3 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("JPistolCounter", 0, "ReloadEnd")
        PIS3 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Clip", 1, 1)
        goto ReloadEnd
        PIS3 A 0 A_TakeInventory("Clip", 1)
        PIS3 A 0 A_GiveInventory("JPistolCounter", 1)
        goto ReloadLoop

      ReloadEnd:
        PIS3 C 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/jpistol3/load", CHAN_WEAPON)
        PIS3 C 15 offset(0, 70)
        PIS3 C 2 offset(0, 60)
        PIS3 C 2 offset(0, 50)
        PIS3 C 2 offset(0, 40)
        PIS3 A 2
        goto Ready

      NoReload:
        PIS3 A 1
        PIS3 A 0 A_ReFire
        goto Ready

      Spawn:
        PWFL A -1   // same as Powerful's sprite
        stop
    }
}

        goto Fire2

        S2WG Z -1
        stop
    }

/home/edrik/projects/jkemod2/pk3/decorate/weapons/jshotgun.txt:

actor JShotgun : Weapon
{
    +AMMO_OPTIONAL
    +NOALERT

    Weapon.SelectionOrder 430
    Weapon.AmmoUse1 1
    Weapon.AmmoGive1 16
    Weapon.AmmoGive2 12
    Weapon.AmmoType1 "JShellCounter"
    Weapon.AmmoType2 "Shell"

    Inventory.PickupMessage "$JKE_PK_JSHOTGUN"
    Obituary "$JKE_MP_JSHOTGUN"
    States
    {
      Ready:
        DHSG A 1 A_WeaponReady
        Loop
      Deselect:
        DHSG A 1 A_Lower
        Loop
      Select:
        DHSG A 1 A_Raise
        Loop
      Fire:
        DHSG A 0 A_JumpIfNoAmmo("AltFire")

        DHSG A 0 A_AlertMonsters
        DHSG A 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/jshotgun/fire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        DHSF A 0 A_Light1
        DHSF A 3 bright A_FireBullets(3, 3, 10, 7, "BulletPuff", 1)
        DHSF BA 3
        DHSG A 1 A_Light0
        DHSG BCD 3
        DHSG E 3 A_PlaySound("jkemod/jshotgun/pump")
        DHSG E 3 A_FireCustomMissile("ShellCasing", -50, 0, 5, 7)
        DHSG DCBA 3
        DHSG A 0 A_ReFire
        Goto Ready

      AltFire:
        DHSG A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("JShellCounter", 0, "NoReload")
        DHSG A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Shell", 1, "ReloadStart")
        Goto NoReload

      ReloadStart:
        DHSG F 3
        DHSR G 8
        Goto ReloadLoop

      ReloadLoop:
        DHSR A 3
        DHSR B 2
        DHSR C 2
        DHSR D 2 A_PlaySound("jkemod/jshotgun/load", CHAN_WEAPON)
        DHSR E 1
        DHSR E 0
        DHSR E 0 A_TakeInventory("Shell", 1)
        DHSR E 0 A_GiveInventory("JShellCounter", 1)
        DHSR E 1
        DHSR F 2 A_JumpIfInventory("MainFired", 1, "ReloadEnd")
        DHSR G 3
        DHSR G 0 A_JumpIfInventory("JShellCounter", 8, "ReloadEnd")
        DHSR G 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Shell", 1, "ReloadLoop")
        Goto ReloadEnd

      ReloadEnd:
        DHSR H 5  A_PlaySound("jkemod/jshotgun/pump", CHAN_WEAPON)
        DHSR G 8
        DHSG F 3
        Goto Ready

      NoReload:
        DHSR A 0
        goto Ready

      Spawn:
        DHSP A -1
        Stop
    }
}

actor JShellCounter: Ammo
{
    +IGNORESKILL
    Inventory.Amount 1
    Inventory.MaxAmount 8

    Ammo.BackpackAmount 0
    Ammo.BackpackMaxAmount 8
}



/home/edrik/projects/jkemod2/pk3/decorate/weapons/jsniperrifle.txt:

actor JSniperRifle : Weapon
{
    +WEAPON.NOAUTOAIM
    Weapon.SelectionOrder 500
    Weapon.AmmoUse1 1
    Weapon.AmmoGive 15
    Weapon.AmmoType1 "JSniperAmmo"
    Inventory.PickupMessage "$JKE_PK_JSNIPERRIFLE"
    Obituary "$JKE_MP_JSNIPERRIFLE"
    States
    {
      Deselect:
        SNIP A 0 A_ZoomFactor(1.0, ZOOM_INSTANT)
        SNIP A 1 A_Lower

      Select:
        SNIP AAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_Raise
        SPRL A 4 A_PlaySound("jkemod/jsniperrifle/load", CHAN_WEAPON)
        SPRL B 4
        SPRL C 4
        SPRL D 4
        SPRL E 4
        Goto Ready

      Ready:
        SNIP A 0 A_TakeInventory("JZoomed")
        SNIP A 1 A_WeaponReady
        Loop

      Fire:
        SNIP B 0 A_Light1
        SNIP B 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/jsniperrifle/fire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        SNIP B 0 A_JumpIfInventory("JZoomed", 1, "ZoomedFire")
        goto UnzoomedFire

      UnzoomedFire:
        SNIP B 3 bright A_FireBullets(12, 12, -1, 100, "JSniperPuff", 1)
        goto FireEnd

      ZoomedFire:
        SNIP B 0 A_ZoomFactor(1.0, ZOOM_INSTANT)
        SNIP B 3 bright A_FireBullets(0, 0, -1, 130, "JSniperPuff", 1)
        goto FireEnd


      FireEnd:
        SNIP C 6 A_Light0
        SNIP A 6
        SPRL A 4 A_PlaySound("jkemod/jsniperrifle/load", CHAN_WEAPON)
        SPRL B 4
        SPRL C 4
        SPRL D 4
        SPRL E 4
        SPRL E 0 A_FireCustomMissile("AssaultCasing", -65, 0, 5, 6)
        SNIP A 8
        Goto Ready

      AltFire:
        SNIP A 0 A_GiveInventory("JZoomed")
        SNIP A 0 A_ZoomFactor(5.0, ZOOM_INSTANT)

        SNIP A 1 A_WeaponReady
        SNIP A 1 A_ReFire

        SNIP A 0 A_ZoomFactor(1.0, ZOOM_INSTANT)
        Goto Ready

      Spawn:
        SNRL A -1
        Stop
    }
}

{
    Inventory.MaxAmount 1
    +UNDROPPABLE
}

actor JSniperPuff: BulletPuff
{
    +NOEXTREMEDEATH
}

actor " M16 ": Weapon
{
    Scale 0.2
    +AMMO_OPTIONAL
    +NOALERT

    weapon.selectionorder 400

    weapon.AmmoGive1 80
    Weapon.AmmoGive2 80
    weapon.AmmoType1 "M16Counter"
    Weapon.AmmoType2 "Clip"
    weapon.AmmoUse1 1

    Inventory.PickupMessage "$JKE_PK_M16"
    Obituary "$JKE_MP_M16"

    States
    {
      Select:
        RIFL A 1 A_Raise
        Loop
      Deselect:
        RIFL A 1 A_Lower
        Loop

      Ready:
        RIFL A 1 A_WeaponReady
        Loop
      Fire:
        RIFL A 0 A_JumpIfNoAmmo("AltFire")
        RIFL A 0 A_AlertMonsters
        RIFL B 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/m16/fire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        RIFL B 0 bright A_FireBullets(0.75, 0.75, 1, 8, "BulletPuff", 1)
        RIFL B 2 bright A_Light1
        RIFL C 2 A_FireCustomMissile("AssaultCasing", -55, 0, 8)
        RIFL D 0 A_ReFire
        RIFL D 3 A_Light0
        RIFL E 3
        Goto Ready

      AltFire:
      ReloadBegin:
        RIFL A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("M16Counter", 0, "NoReload")
        RIFL A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Clip", 1, 1)
        Goto NoReload

        RIFL GHI 5
        RIFL J 5 A_PlaySound("jkemod/m16/out", CHAN_WEAPON)
        RIFL K 5
        RIFL L 10
        RIFL KJI 5
        goto ReloadLoop

      ReloadLoop:
        RIFL I 0 A_TakeInventory("Clip", 1)
        RIFL I 0 A_GiveInventory("M16Counter", 1)
        RIFL I 0 A_JumpIfInventory("M16Counter", 0, "ReloadEnd")
        RIFL I 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Clip", 1, "ReloadLoop")
        goto ReloadEnd

      ReloadEnd:
        RIFL M 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/m16/in", CHAN_WEAPON)
        RIFL MNOPQRST 4
        Goto Ready

      NoReload:
        RIFL A 1
        RIFL A 0 A_ReFire
        goto Ready

      Spawn:
        RIFL Z -1
        stop
    }
}

actor FistCounter: Inventory
{
    Inventory.MaxAmount 7
}

actor " Mighty Fist ": Weapon
{
    +UNDROPPABLE
    +NOALERT
    +WEAPON.MELEEWEAPON
    +WEAPON.WIMPY_WEAPON

    Weapon.Kickback 0
    Weapon.SelectionOrder 1800

    Inventory.PickupMessage "$JKE_PK_MIGHTYFIST"
    Obituary "$JKE_MP_MIGHTYFIST"

    States
    {
      Select:
        MFST A 0 A_Raise
        MFST A 1 A_Raise
        loop

      Deselect:
        MFST A 0 A_Lower
        MFST A 1 A_Lower
        loop

      Ready:
        MFST A 0 A_TakeInventory("FistCounter")
        MFST A 1 A_WeaponReady
        Loop

      Fire:
        MFST A 0 A_GiveInventory("FistCounter")
        MFST A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("FistCounter", 7, "Fire7")
        MFST A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("FistCounter", 6, "Fire6")
        MFST A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("FistCounter", 5, "Fire5")
        MFST A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("FistCounter", 4, "Fire4")
        MFST A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("FistCounter", 3, "Fire3")
        MFST A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("FistCounter", 2, "Fire2")
        goto Fire1

      Fire1:
        MFST A 0
        MFST B 3
        MFST C 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/mightyfist/fire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        MFST C 2
        MFST D 2 A_CustomPunch(15, 1, 0, "MightyBulletPuff")
        MFST C 2
        MFST B 3
        MFST L 2
        TNT1 A 5 A_ReFire
        goto Ready

      Fire2:
        MFST E 3
        MFST F 2
        MFST G 1
        MFST F 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/mightyfist/fire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        MFST F 2
        MFST E 3 A_CustomPunch(15, 1, 0, "MightyBulletPuff")
        MFST L 3
        TNT1 A 5 A_ReFire
        goto Ready

      Fire3:
        MFST B 3
        MFST C 2
        MFST H 2
        MFST I 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/mightyfist/fire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        MFST I 1
        MFST J 1 A_CustomPunch(15, 1, 0, "MightyBulletPuff")
        MFST K 2
        TNT1 A 1
        TNT1 A 5 A_ReFire
        goto Ready

      Fire4:
        PUNC F 2
        PUNC G 2
        PUNC H 2
        PUNC I 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/mightyfist/fire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        PUNC I 2
        PUNC J 1 A_Punch
        PUNC K 1
        PUNC L 1
        TNT1 A 5 A_ReFire
        goto Ready

      Fire5:
        PUNA M 2
        PUNA N 2
        PUNA O 2
        PUNA P 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/mightyfist/fire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        PUNA P 2
        PUNA Q 1 A_Punch
        PUNA R 1
        PUNA S 1
        PUNA T 1
        TNT1 A 5 A_ReFire
        goto Ready

      Fire6:
        KEKE A 3
        KEKE B 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/mightyfist/fire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        KEKE B 2 A_CustomPunch(20, 1, 0, "MightyBulletPuff")
        KEKE A 6
        TNT1 A 5 A_ReFire
        goto Ready

      Fire7:
        KEKE C 3
        KEKE D 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/mightyfist/fire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        KEKE D 3 A_CustomPunch(25, 1, 0, "MightyBulletPuff")
        KEKE C 5
        TNT1 A 15
        goto Ready

      Spawn:
        TNT1 A -1
        stop
    }
}


actor MightyBulletPuff: BulletPuff
{
    SeeSound "jkemod/mightyfist/hit"
}
