/home/edrik/projects/jkemod2/pk3/decorate/weapons/multigun.txt:

actor " Multigun ": Weapon
{

    Weapon.AmmoType1 "ExplosiveAmmo"
    Weapon.AmmoUse1 1
    Weapon.AmmoGive1 10

    +NOAUTOFIRE
    +NOALERT
    Weapon.SelectionOrder 800

    Inventory.PickupMessage "$JKE_PK_MULTIGUN"
    Obituary "$JKE_MP_MULTIGUN"

    States
    {
      Select:
        SBRG A 1 A_Raise
        loop

      Deselect:
        SBRG A 1 A_Lower
        loop

      Ready:
        SBRG A 1 A_WeaponReady
        Loop

      Fire:
        SBRG A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("MultigunFired", 1, "GenericLoad")

        SBRG A 0 A_AlertMonsters
        SBRG A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("MultigunMode", 2, "FlameFire")
        SBRG A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("MultigunMode", 1, "IceFire")
        goto RocketFire

      RocketFire:
        SBRG A 0 A_FireCustomMissile("MultigunRocket", 0, 1, 4, 1)
        goto GenericFire

      IceFire:
        SBRG A 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/multigun/icefire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        SBRG A 0 A_FireCustomMissile("MultigunIce", 0, 1, 4, 4)
        SBRG A 0 A_FireCustomMissile("MultigunIce", 6, 0, 4, 1)
        SBRG A 0 A_FireCustomMissile("MultigunIce", -5, 0, 4, 3)
        SBRG A 0 A_FireCustomMissile("MultigunIce", 2, 0, 4, 5)
        SBRG A 0 A_FireCustomMissile("MultigunIce", -2, 0, 4, 0)
        SBRG A 0 A_FireCustomMissile("MultigunIce", -4, 0, 4, 2)
        goto GenericFire

      FlameFire:
        SBRG A 0 A_FireCustomMissile("MultigunFlameGrenade", 0, 1, 4, 2)
        goto GenericFire


      GenericFire:
        SBRG A 0 A_GiveInventory("MultigunFired")
        SBRG BC 3 bright
        SBRG D 3
        SBRG A 2
        goto Ready

      GenericLoad:
        SBRG EF 2
        SBRG A 0 A_TakeInventory("MultigunFired")
        SBRG G 4 A_PlaySound("jkemod/multigun/load", CHAN_WEAPON)
        SBRG FED 2
        goto Ready

      AltFire:
        SBRG A 0 A_TakeInventory("MultigunFired")
        SBRG A 0 ACS_ExecuteAlways(875)
        SBRG EFGG 2
        SBRR A 1
        SBRR BCDEFGMMMH 2
        goto AltSecond

      AltSecond:
        SBRR IJ 2
        SBRR K 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/multigun/switch", CHAN_WEAPON)
        SBRR KLKJIH 2
        SBRR A 0 A_ReFire
        SBRR GFEDBA 2
        SBRG GFE 2
        goto Ready

      AltHold:
        SBRG A 0 ACS_ExecuteAlways(875)
        goto AltSecond


      Spawn:
        SBRG Z -1
        stop
    }
}

actor MultigunFired: Inventory
{
    Inventory.MaxAmount 1
    +UNDROPPABLE
}

actor MultigunMode: Inventory
{
    Inventory.MaxAmount 2
    +UNDROPPABLE
}

actor P-200 : Weapon
{
    Weapon.AmmoType1 "Cell"
    Weapon.AmmoType2 "Cell"
    Weapon.AmmoUse1 12
    Weapon.AmmoUse2 1
    Weapon.AmmoGive 50

    Weapon.SelectionOrder 900
    Inventory.PickupMessage "$JKE_PK_P200"
    Obituary "$JKE_MP_P200"
    States
    {
      Select:
        P200 A 1 A_Raise
        loop
      Deselect:
        P200 A 1 A_Lower
        loop

      Ready:
        P200 A 1 A_WeaponReady
        Loop

      Fire:
        P200 B 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/p200/fire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        P200 B 0 A_FireCustomMissile("P200Shot", random(-50, 50)/10.0, 1, 5, -1, 0, random(-30, 30)/10.0)
        P200 BBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBB 0 A_FireCustomMissile("P200Shot", random(-50, 50)/10.0, 0, 5, -1, 0, random(-30, 30)/10.0)
        P200 BC 0 A_GunFlash
        P200 BCDEFGGGGGGGGGG 2
        P200 A 1 A_ReFire
        goto Ready

/home/edrik/projects/jkemod2/pk3/decorate/weapons/quadshot.txt:

actor QuadShot: Weapon
{
    Weapon.AmmoType1 "QuadShotCounter"
    Weapon.AmmoType2 "Shell"
    Weapon.AmmoUse1 1
    Weapon.AmmoUse2 4
    Weapon.AmmoGive1 1
    Weapon.AmmoGive2 16

    Weapon.SelectionOrder 1000

    +AMMO_OPTIONAL
    +ALT_AMMO_OPTIONAL

    Inventory.PickupMessage "$JKE_PK_QUADSHOT"
    Obituary "$JKE_MP_QUADSHOT"

    States
    {
      Select:
        QSHT A 1 A_Raise
        loop
      Deselect:
        QSHT A 1 A_Lower
        loop

      Ready:
        QSHT A 1 A_WeaponReady
        loop

      Fire:
        GSHT A 0 A_JumpIfNoAmmo("AltFire")

        QSHT A 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/quadshot/fire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        QSHT A 0 A_FireBullets(5, 5, 40, 7, "Bulletpuff", 1)
        QSHT B 1 bright offset(0, 40) A_Light2
        QSHT C 5 bright offset(0, 44)
        QSHT B 2 bright A_Light1
        QSHT B 1 bright offset(0, 42)
        QSHT A 1
        QSHT A 1 offset(0, 40)
        QSHT A 1 offset(0, 38)
        QSHT A 1 offset(0, 36)
        QSHT A 1 offset(0, 34)
        QSHT A 0 A_Light0
        QSHT A 24 offset(0, 32)
        goto Ready

      AltFire:
        QSHT A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("QuadShotCounter", 0, "NoLoad")
        QSHT A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Shell", 4, 1)
        goto NoLoad

        QSHT A 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/quadshot/load", CHAN_WEAPON)
        QSHT DE 4
        QSHT A 0 A_GiveInventory("QuadShotCounter", 1)
        QSHT A 0 A_TakeInventory("Shell", 4)
        QSHT A 8
        goto Ready

      NoLoad:
        QSHT A 1
        goto Ready


      Spawn:
        QSHT Z -1
        stop
    }
}


actor QuadShotCounter: Ammo
{
    Inventory.MaxAmount 4
    +IGNORESKILL
}

actor Spitfirer: Weapon
{
    Weapon.AmmoType1 "Clip"
    Weapon.AmmoType2 "ExplosiveAmmo"
    Weapon.AmmoUse1 1
    Weapon.AmmoUse2 1
    Weapon.AmmoGive1 70
    Weapon.AmmoGive2 4

    Weapon.SelectionOrder 900

    Inventory.PickupMessage "$JKE_PK_SPITFIRER"
    Obituary "$JKE_MP_SPITFIRER"

    States
    {
      Select:
        SPFR A 1 A_Raise
        loop

      Deselect:
        SPFR A 1 A_Lower
        loop

      Ready:
        SPFR A 1 A_WeaponReady
        Loop

      Fire:
        SPFR A 0 A_GunFlash
        SPFR A 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/spitfirer/fire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        SPFR A 0 A_FireCustomMissile("PistolCasing", -40, 0, 0, 6)
        SPFR B 2 A_FireBullets(1.5, 1.5, 1, 8, "BulletPuff")
        SPFR A 1
        SPFR A 0 A_ReFire
        goto Ready

      AltFire:
        SPFR B 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/spitfirer/altfire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        SPFR B 1 A_FireCustomMissile("SpitfirerGrenade", 0, 1, 2, 3)
        SPFR G 1
        SPFR I 10
        SPFR I 10 A_PlaySound("jkemod/spitfirer/open", CHAN_WEAPON)
        SPFR HGEB 1
        goto Ready


      Flash:
        SPFR A 0 A_Jump(255, "Flash1", "Flash2")
        goto LightDone

      Flash1:
        SPFR J 2 bright A_Light1
        goto LightDone

      Flash2:
        SPFR K 2 bright A_Light1
        goto LightDone


      Spawn:
        SPFR Z -1
        stop
    }
}

actor " Striker ": Weapon
{
    +AMMO_OPTIONAL
    Weapon.AmmoGive1 16
    Weapon.AmmoGive2 16
    Weapon.AmmoType1 "StrikerCounter"
    Weapon.AmmoType2 "Shell"
    Weapon.AmmoUse1 1
    Weapon.SelectionOrder 600
    Scale 0.6

    Inventory.PickupMessage "$JKE_PK_STRIKER"
    Obituary "$JKE_MP_STRIKER"
    States
    {
      Select:
        STKK A 1 A_Raise
        loop

      Deselect:
        STKK A 1 A_Lower
        loop

      Ready:
        STKK A 1 A_WeaponReady
        Loop

      Fire:
        STKK A 0 A_JumpIfNoAmmo("AltFire")

        STKK A 0 A_FireCustomMissile("ShellCasing", -48, 0, 3, 6)
        STKK A 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/striker/fire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        STKK A 0 A_FireBullets(3, 3, 10, 5, "Bulletpuff")
        STKF AB 2 bright A_Light1
        STKK A 4 A_Light0
        goto Ready

      AltFire:
        STKK A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("StrikerCounter", 0, "NoReload")
        STKK A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Shell", 1, "ReloadStart")
        goto NoReload

      ReloadStart:
        STKK B 3
        STKR A 10
        STKR B 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/striker/out", CHAN_WEAPON)
        STKR B 3
        STKR CDEFGHIIIIIIIIIIHGFEDC 2
        goto ReloadLoop

      ReloadLoop:
        STKK A 0 A_TakeInventory("Shell", 1)
        STKK A 0 A_GiveInventory("StrikerCounter", 1)
        STKK A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("StrikerCounter", 0, "ReloadEnd")
        STKK A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Shell", 1, "ReloadLoop")
        goto ReloadEnd

      ReloadEnd:
        STKR B 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/striker/in", CHAN_WEAPON)
        STKR B 3
        STKR J 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/striker/load", CHAN_WEAPON)
        STKR JJJKKJJJ 2
        STKK B 3
        STKK A 4
        goto Ready

      NoReload:
        STKK A 1
        STKK A 0 A_ReFire
        goto Ready

      Spawn:
        STKK Z -1
        stop
    }
}

{
    +IGNORESKILL
    Inventory.MaxAmount 16
}



/home/edrik/projects/jkemod2/pk3/decorate/weapons/supershotnuke.txt:

actor " Super Shotnuke ": Weapon
{
    Weapon.AmmoType1 "NukeShell"
    Weapon.AmmoType2 "SuperShotNukeCounter"
    Weapon.AmmoUse1 0
    Weapon.AmmoUse2 0
    Weapon.AmmoGive1 2
    Weapon.AmmoGive2 0

    Weapon.SelectionOrder 800
    Weapon.Kickback 2000

    Inventory.PickupMessage "$JKE_PK_SUPERSHOTNUKE"
    Obituary "$JKE_MP_SUPERSHOTNUKE"

    States
    {
      Select:
        PKS2 A 1 A_Raise
        loop
      Deselect:
        PKS2 A 1 A_Lower
        loop

      Ready:
        PKS2 A 1 A_WeaponReady
        Loop

      Fire:
        PKS2 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SuperShotNukeCounter", 0, "RealFire")
        goto NoLoad

      RealFire:
        PKS2 A 0 A_Stop
        PKS2 A 0 ThrustThing(angle*256/360, 64*-cos(pitch), 0, 0)
        PKS2 A 0 ThrustThingZ(0, 256*sin(pitch), 0, 1)
        PKS2 A 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/supershotnuke/fire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        PKS2 A 0 A_TakeInventory("SuperShotNukeCounter", 10)
        PKS2 A 0 A_FireBullets(16, 4, 1000, 250, "SuperShotNukePuff", 1)
        PKS2 C 1 bright
        PKS2 E 140
        PKS2 D 35
        PKS2 C 18
        PKS2 B 9
        Goto Ready

      AltFire:
        PKS2 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SuperShotNukeCounter", 0, "NoLoad")
        PKS2 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("NukeShell", 2, "Load")
        Goto NoLoad

      Load:
        PKS2 BCD 2
        PKS2 E 6
        PKS2 F 3 A_PlaySound("jkemod/supershotnuke/open", CHAN_WEAPON)
        PKS2 GH 2
        PKS2 I 1
        NKS2 JK 1
        PKS2 L 0 A_GiveInventory("SuperShotNukeCounter", 2)
        PKS2 L 0 A_TakeInventory("NukeShell", 2)
        NKS2 L 3 A_PlaySound("jkemod/supershotnuke/load", CHAN_WEAPON)
        NKS2 MN 2
        NKS2 OP 1
        PKS2 Q 1
        PKS2 R 0 A_JumpIfInventory("AltFired", 1, "CheckKeepLoading")
        goto BackToLoad

      BackToLoad:
        PKS2 R 3 A_PlaySound("jkemod/supershotnuke/close", CHAN_WEAPON)
        PKS2 S 3
        PKS2 T 1
        Goto Ready

      CheckKeepLoading:
        PKS2 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SuperShotNukeCounter", 0, "BackToLoad")
        PKS2 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("NukeShell", 2, "KeepLoading")
        goto BackToLoad

      KeepLoading:
        PKS2 R 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/supershotnuke/close", CHAN_WEAPON)
        Goto Load


      NoFire:
      NoLoad:
        PKS2 A 1
        PKS2 A 0 A_ReFire
        goto Ready

      Spawn:
        SGN2 A -1
        stop
    }
}

    Weapon.AmmoGive2 50

    Inventory.PickupMessage "$JKE_PK_UZI"

    States

      Select:
        UZIC AAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_Raise
        UZIC BC 3
        UZIC D 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/uzi/cock", CHAN_WEAPON)
        UZIC DEFBA 3
        goto Ready

      Deselect:
        UZIG AA 0 A_Lower
        UZIG A 1
        loop

      Ready:
        UZIG A 1 A_WeaponReady
        Loop


      Fire:
        UZIG A 0 A_JumpIfNoAmmo("AltFire")

        UZIG B 1 bright A_Light1
        UZIG C 0 A_FireCustomMissile("PistolCasing", -40, 0, 2, 6)
        UZIG C 1 bright A_FireBullets(2, 2, 1, 6, "BulletPuff")
        UZIG D 1 bright A_Light0
        UZIG A 3 A_ReFire
        goto Ready


      AltFire:
        UZIG A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("UziCounter", 0, "NoReload")
        UZIG A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Clip", 1, "ReloadStart")
        goto NoReload

      ReloadStart:
        UZIR A 4
        UZIR B 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/uzi/open", CHAN_WEAPON)
        UZIR BCD 3
        UZIR E 25
        UZIR F 3
        goto ReloadLoop

      ReloadLoop:
        UZIC A 0 A_TakeInventory("Clip", 1)
        UZIC A 0 A_GiveInventory("UziCounter", 1)
        UZIC A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("UziCounter", 0, "ReloadEnd")
        UZIC A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Clip", 1, "ReloadLoop")
        goto ReloadEnd

      ReloadEnd:
        UZIR G 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/uzi/load", CHAN_WEAPON)
        UZIR GH 3
        UZIG A 3
        UZIC BC 3
        UZIC D 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/uzi/cock", CHAN_WEAPON)
        UZIC DEFB 3
        UZIC A 2
        goto Ready

      NoReload:
        UZIG A 1
        UZIG A 0 A_ReFire
        goto Ready

      Spawn:
        UZIP A -1
        stop
    }
}

        LIGF B 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/voltgun/fire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        LIGF B 0 A_RailAttack(70, 2, 1, none, "EF BF 00", 1, 8)
        LIGF B 2 bright
        LIGF A 2 bright
        LIGG A 2 A_Light0
        LIGG A 2
        LIGG A 5 A_ReFire
        goto Ready
      AltFire:
        LIGF A 0 A_Light2
        LIGF B 0 A_PlaySound("jkemod/voltgun/altfire", CHAN_WEAPON)
        LIGF B 0 A_RailAttack(50, 2, 1, none, "FF FF 00", 1, 5)
        LIGF B 0 A_RailAttack(70, 2, 0, none, "FF AF 00", 1, 8)
        LIGF B 0 A_RailAttack(90, 2, 0, none, "CC CC FF", 1, 11)
        LIGF B 2 bright
        LIGF A 2 bright
        LIGG A 34 A_Light0
        LIGG A 0 A_ReFire
        goto Ready
      Spawn:
        LIGH A -1
        stop
    }
}

actor " Zen Fist ": Weapon

    +UNDROPPABLE
    +NOALERT
    +WEAPON.MELEEWEAPON
    +WEAPON.WIMPY_WEAPON

    Weapon.SelectionOrder 1000
    Weapon.Kickback 100

    Inventory.PickupMessage "$JKE_PK_ZENFIST"
    Obituary "$JKE_MP_ZENFIST"

    States
    {
      Ready:
        FIST A 1 A_WeaponReady
        Loop
      Deselect:
        FIST A 0 A_Lower
        FIST A 1 A_Lower
        Loop
      Select:
        FIST A 0 A_Raise
        FIST A 1 A_Raise
        Loop
      Fire:
        FIST B 0 A_JumpIfInventory("PunchSide",1,6)
        FIST B 2
        FIST C 3 A_Punch
        FIST BA 2
        FIST A 0 A_GiveInventory("PunchSide")
        Goto Ready
        FIST D 2
        FIST E 3 A_Punch
        FIST DA 2
        FIST A 0 A_TakeInventory("PunchSide")
        Goto Ready
      AltFire:
        KICK ABC 2
        KICK D 3 A_CustomPunch(40,1,0,"ZenFistPuff")
        KICK EDCB 2
        KICK A 2 A_ReFire
        Goto Ready
    }
}

actor Dukepistol : Weapon
{
    +AMMO_OPTIONAL
    Inventory.PickupMessage "You got Dn's pistol"
    Weapon.AmmoGive1 40
    Weapon.AmmoGive2 40
    Weapon.AmmoType1 "Dukeclip"
    Weapon.AmmoType2 "Clip"
    Weapon.AmmoUse1 1
    Weapon.SelectionOrder 1300
    Obituary "-"
    AttackSound "weapons/dukefire"
    States
    {
      Ready:
        DN6G A 1 A_WeaponReady
        Loop
      Select:
        DN6G A 0 A_Raise
        DN6G A 1 A_Raise
        Loop
      Deselect:
        DN6G A 0 A_Lower
        DN6G A 1 A_Lower
        loop
      Fire:
        DN6G A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Dukeclip", 1, 2)
        DN6G A 0
        goto AltFire
        DN6F A 2 bright A_FireBullets(3, 3, 1, 6, "Bulletpuff", 1)
        DN6F B 1 bright
        DN6G B 1 bright
        DN6G C 0 A_FireCustomMissile("AssaultCasing", 55, 0, 1, 7)
        DN6G C 2
        DN6G B 1
        DN6G A 1
        DN6G A 0 A_ReFire
        goto Ready
      AltFire:
        DN6G A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Dukeclip", 20, 2)
        DN6G A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Clip", 1, 2)
        DN6G A 0
        goto Ready
        DN6R A 6
        DN6R B 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/dossgbopn", CHAN_WEAPON)
        DN6R B 3
        DN6R C 2
        DN6R D 2
        DN6R E 2
        DN6R F 3
        DN6R G 20
        DN6R H 3
        DN6R I 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/dossgload", CHAN_WEAPON)
        DN6R I 2
        DN6R J 2
        DN6R K 2
        DN6R L 2
        DN6R M 2
        DN6R N 3
        DN6R O 3
        DN6G A 3
        DN6G A 0
        DN6G A 0 A_TakeInventory("Clip", 1)
        DN6G A 0 A_GiveInventory("Dukeclip", 1)
        DN6G A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Dukeclip", 20, 4)
        DN6G A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Clip", 1, 2)
        DN6G A 0
        goto AltFire+28
        DN6G A 0
        goto AltFire+22
        DN6G A 1
        goto Ready
      Spawn:
        1911 A -1
        stop
    }
